# Session Log ‚Äî 2026-07

Append-only. Newest entry at the bottom. One entry per session, written by
the chronicler BEFORE the session's final commit so the entry rides in it.
Format: `## <date> ‚Äî <issue/trigger> ‚Äî <outcome>`, then what was
attempted/shipped (commit hash), ratchet movement, decisions, surprises,
friction, next.

## 2026-07-06 ‚Äî bootstrap ‚Äî repo scaffolded

- Shipped: module scaffold, docs (STYLE/PRINCIPLES/ARCHITECTURE/PLAN/
  WORKFLOW/ROUTINES), local specs (5 W3C documents, HTML + generated
  Markdown), spec tooling (fetchspecs/spec2md/rulecat/hfnextract), W3C
  suite submodule, conformance ratchet contract, package doc.go contracts,
  agent personas and commands, lint gate, GitHub labels/milestones and the
  seed `ready` issues for M1.
- Ratchet: no lanes yet ‚Äî the first `datatypes` lane lands with M3.
- Decisions: docs-only bootstrap (all library Go code is written by the
  develop loop against the committed contracts); builtin wiring =
  backend-neutral generated TypeSpec table + per-primitive Mappings +
  capability discovery on values + Seed/Override composition; one regex
  engine with two flavors; no Make ‚Äî Go subcommands and `go tool` only.
- Next: `/plan` to review the seeded M1 issues, then the develop loop.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî issue #1 ‚Äî ratchet mechanics shipped

- Shipped: conformance/expectations.go ‚Äî the M1 mechanics contract from
  conformance/doc.go: Status (closed pass/fail type via Pass/Fail + derived
  IsPass), LoadExpectations (missing file => empty lane), Compare (Delta with
  Improved/Regressed/New/Vanished, all sorted), Ratchet (upward-only merge;
  refuses entirely on any Regressed or Vanished; inputs never mutated),
  WriteExpectations (sorted, atomic temp+rename, byte-stable). Full unit
  coverage in conformance/expectations_test.go incl. both refusal paths and a
  byte-stability test from randomized insertion order.
- Spec: n/a ‚Äî process infrastructure per conformance/doc.go and the oracle
  grounding (.agent/grounding-issue-1.md). Errors are plain wrapped Go errors
  (STYLE E1), not *xsderr.Error.
- Ratchet: unchanged (no lanes populated yet; mechanics only).
- Decisions: expectation-file errors are fmt.Errorf/%w with file+line context,
  not xsderr; duplicate case IDs in a lane file are a load error.
- Next: the TestConformance suite runner (separate issue) that drives these
  mechanics against testdata/xsdtests.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî meta (interactive) ‚Äî branch lifecycle needs no ref deletion

- Shipped: workflow restructure so agents never hit a blocked git
  operation. Cloud containers cannot delete or force-push remote refs
  (issue #1's landing left `wip/issue-1` stranded; MCP/`gh` were also
  unavailable in that run). Landing now goes through a PR squash-merged
  via the GitHub Merge API (`Closes #<N>` in the body; repo setting
  "Automatically delete head branches" enabled ‚Äî the system's only ref
  deletion). Parking retires the branch in place under `needs-replan`
  (the `parked/issue-<N>-<ts>` rename+delete is gone; branch scheme is
  down to three kinds). Re-planned issues are superseded by a new issue
  number so retired names are never contended. Resumes merge main in
  instead of rebasing (a rebased branch cannot be pushed without
  force). Touched WORKFLOW/ROUTINES/PRINCIPLES/CLAUDE.md, develop.md,
  arbiter.md; container limits stated once, in ROUTINES.md.
- Ratchet: unchanged (docs only).
- Decisions: sessions only ever CREATE refs; branch-namespace GC is
  report-only for agents. `GITHUB_PAT` now set in the routine env for
  the MCP channel. ROUTINES.md schedule table now lists UTC cron times.
- Next: watch the next /develop routine land via the Merge API
  end-to-end; confirm the cloud channel can open + squash-merge a PR.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî issue #2 ‚Äî hfn‚ÜíTypeSpec generator emits builtin/gen_typespec.go

- Shipped: the M1 builtin data table. `tools/hfnextract/builtins` parses all
  49 builtins from the local specs (per-type Facets prose subsections in
  ¬ß3.3/¬ß3.4 + each type's opening definition sentence, cross-checked against
  Appendix F.1); `tools/typespecgen` maps that to Go and emits
  builtin/gen_typespec.go (`var Types []TypeSpec`, 49 rows, spec order).
  Closed value types (Variety, Fundamental enums, Facet) hand-written in
  builtin/typespec.go; the generated file is data-only. Wired to
  `go generate` via builtin/gen.go; typespecgen registered in go.mod's tool
  block. Tests: row count 49, primitive set, list variety, precisionDecimal
  applicable facets, plus a determinism + committed-up-to-date guard in
  typespecgen. Full gate green; `go generate ./...` twice byte-identical.
- Spec: ¬ß3.2.2/¬ß3.3/¬ß3.4 (type defs), ¬ß4.1.6 dummy-def (primitive base),
  ¬ß4.2 + Appendix F.1 (fundamental facets), ¬ß4.1.5 cos-applicable-facets,
  xsd-precisionDecimal.md ¬ß3 (totalDigits/maxScale/minScale).
- Ratchet: unchanged (new package, no conformance lanes touched).
- Decisions / DEVIATION FROM ISSUE WORDING: the issue's acceptance said "19
  primitives with Base == anySimpleType". Per ¬ß4.1.6 dummy-def (oracle-
  confirmed) every primitive's {base type definition} is **anyAtomicType**,
  not anySimpleType; anySimpleType is only anyAtomicType's base. Implemented
  spec-correct (Base=anyAtomicType) rather than encode a spec error into the
  ratchet. precisionDecimal is therefore a 20th primitive by Base; the test
  checks the classic 19 by name AND asserts 20 IsPrimitive rows. The earlier
  GROUNDING comment's "anySimpleType for primitives" was a misread of ¬ß4.1.6.
- Surprises: three 1.1 types (yearMonthDuration/dayTimeDuration/dateTimeStamp)
  state their base only via "¬∑derived¬∑ from [X]", not the "¬∑base type¬∑ of X
  is Y" sentence; `language` links its own name instead of bolding it ‚Äî the
  base regex tolerates both. anyAtomicType has empty {facets} and empty
  {fundamental facets}; the Fundamental enums carry an Absent zero to model
  it. TypeSpec dropped the sketch's separate `Applicable` field (derivable
  from Facets, STYLE D3) and added `Item` for list types.
- Next: value.Backend + builtin.Seed composition (later issue) consumes this
  table; Appendix E hfn lex/canonical maps are out of scope here.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî issue #2 warden REVISE ‚Äî Variety/Fundamental illegal-states repair

- Shipped: warden repair round on the builtin API. Two blocking [T1] findings
  resolved: (1) `Variety` uint8 enum + `TypeSpec.Item` replaced by a sealed
  sum (`type Variety interface{ variety() }`, branches `Atomic struct{}` and
  `List struct{ Item string }`) so an item type cannot exist without list-ness
  (STYLE T1/T2); (2) the four fundamental enums dropped their `*Absent` zero
  members and moved to `iota+1` (invalid zero ‚Üí unset field is a caught bug),
  and `TypeSpec.Fundamental` became `*Fundamental` ‚Äî nil is the empty
  {fundamental facets} that only anyAtomicType carries, collapsing the
  all-or-nothing into one structural fact so a partial mix is unrepresentable.
- Emitter (tools/typespecgen): `varietyConst`‚Üí`varietyLit` emits `Atomic{}` /
  `List{Item: "..."}`; `fundamental` emits `&Fundamental{...}` or "" (skip the
  field, leaving nil) when all four spec tokens are empty; per-field `""‚ÜíAbsent`
  map entries removed so a stray empty token errors instead of silently
  meaning absent. doc.go sketch + prose updated; tests updated to type-assert
  Variety and check `Fundamental == nil`.
- Spec: ¬ß4.1.1 (variety), ¬ß4.2 (fundamental facets), ¬ß4.1.6 anyAtomicType-def
  (empty {fundamental facets}).
- Ratchet: unchanged.
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint all green; `go generate ./...` twice
  byte-identical.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî issue #3 ‚Äî xsderr: Error/Rule/Loc + generated rule catalog

- Shipped on wip/issue-3: implemented the xsderr error currency package
  (error.go) ‚Äî Rule, Loc (with String), Error{Rule,Loc,Msg,Err} rendering
  "loc: [rule] msg", Unwrap for errors.Is/As reach-through, New, Wrap (message
  verbatim + identity preserved), RuleOf/LocOf (errors.As narrowing). gen.go
  wires `//go:generate go tool rulecat`; xsderr/catalog.go committed.
- Fixed tools/rulecat extraction (was `\b(cvc|cos|src)-...`): widened prefix
  family to cvc|cos|src|sic and added a whole-word alternation for the known
  irregular literal IDs (derivation-ok-restriction, sch-props-correct, and the
  xmlschema11-2 facet-restriction rules length-valid-restriction,
  enumeration-valid-restriction, timezone-valid-restriction,
  length-minLength-maxLength). coss-*/ct-* section/property anchors stay out
  (the required "-" after the prefix and whole-word anchoring exclude them).
  Also made rulecat locate the module root itself so the arg-free directive
  works whether `go generate` runs in the repo root or the xsderr package dir.
  Catalog: 132 rules.
- Verdicts: Warden accept-with-notes (no blockers); Arbiter accept ‚Äî full gate
  green, ratchet run confirmed as genuine no-op (pure new infrastructure, no
  lane movement), independently re-verified rule extraction byte-for-byte
  correct against specs (126 prefix-family + 6 irregulars = 132 total, zero
  false positives/negatives).
- Notes for follow-up: (1) doc.go's contract text should explicitly name
  `Loc.String()` in its example list; (2) doc.go cites `cvc-complex-type.2.1`
  as an example Rule but only the base anchor `cvc-complex-type` is catalogued
  (spec sub-clause suffixes aren't catalogued, to be resolved by whichever
  future issue first emits a cvc- Rule citing a sub-clause).
- Spec: n/a (infrastructure; rulecat grounded in xmlschema11-1.md ¬ß2.3, ¬ß3.4.6.3,
  xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß4.3.1.4 ‚Äî see .agent/grounding-issue-3.md).
- Ratchet: unchanged.
- Gate: build/test/vet green; golangci-lint 0 issues; `go generate ./...` twice
  byte-identical (catalog md5 438e0dbb‚Ä¶), tree otherwise clean.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî #5 parser/xmltree package ‚Äî Shipped (plus xsderr.RuleXMLWellFormed sentinel)

- Shipped on wip/issue-5 (commit 50a5e62): `parser/xmltree` streaming XML
  reader with in-scope namespace binding tracking and position reporting.
  Files: `name.go` (`Name` {Space,Local} + fixed `xml:`‚Üí`http://www.w3.org/
  XML/1998/namespace` binding, unexported reserved-prefix consts), `scope.go`
  (immutable persistent namespace-scope chain, `lookup` with implicit `xml`,
  default-namespace fallback, and 1.1-style `xmlns:p=""` undeclaration),
  `node.go` (sealed `Node` sum `*StartElement`/`*EndElement`/`*CharData` +
  `Attribute` value type; `StartElement.LookupPrefix` exposes in-scope
  bindings for QName-valued-content resolution per Datatypes ¬ß3.3.18),
  `reader.go` (`Reader`/`NewReader`/`Token`; `RawToken`-based streaming with
  own namespace resolution, own start/end matching, `posReader` newline
  index + `sort.Search` line/col), `reader_test.go`, `fuzz_test.go`.
  Repair round (commit 1fbe2e4): Added `xsderr.RuleXMLWellFormed = "xml-wf"`
  sentinel Rule for XML well-formedness faults and relocated `IsValidRule`
  from generated `catalog.go` to hand-written `error.go` so the sentinel
  exemption survives `go generate`; updated `tools/rulecat` to emit only the
  ruleCatalog data table; updated all 9 well-formedness error sites in
  `reader.go` to use the sentinel; threaded open tag's Loc through frame
  for better unclosed-element error location reporting.
- Spec: n/a (generic XML/Namespaces-in-XML, not locally specced; only the
  `xml:` fixed binding is generic-XML knowledge ‚Äî oracle grounded in issue #5
  comment). Uses RawToken so unbound prefixes are caught by our own resolver
  and reported as errors, never passed through as namespaces (doc.go contract).
- Verdicts: Warden rejected on one blocking [E1] finding: initial implementation
  used `xsderr.New("", loc, ...)` (empty Rule string) which violates xsderr's
  "exactly one Rule identifies each Error" contract. Mason repair round
  addressed finding by adding RuleXMLWellFormed sentinel and updating all
  well-formedness sites. Arbiter accept ‚Äî full gate green, ratchet unchanged
  (touches no conformance/ files), xsderr foundational change verified sound
  (byte-identical `go generate` output for catalog.go, no other callers of
  IsValidRule broken).
- Decisions: (1) unbound-prefix / mismatched-tag / unclosed / malformed-XML
  errors are XML well-formedness faults, NOT XSD validity violations, so they
  are `*xsderr.Error` with a Loc and the `RuleXMLWellFormed` sentinel (not
  empty) ‚Äî this satisfies xsderr's contract while keeping `xsderr.LocOf`
  working for downstream threading (STYLE E1). (2) Column counts raw BYTES from
  line start, not runes: rune columns would need retained content, violating
  STYLE P4; documented on `locAt`. (3) `RawToken` (not `Token`) is used
  precisely because encoding/xml's `Token` passes unbound prefixes through as
  if they were namespace URIs ‚Äî the exact behavior doc.go forbids. (4)
  Attribute Loc = owning element start, since encoding/xml exposes no
  per-attribute offsets; documented. (5) Exported surface kept minimal (STYLE
  T5): no `InScopeNamespaces` enumerator ‚Äî `LookupPrefix` covers
  QName-valued-content resolution.
- Ratchet: unchanged (new leaf package, no conformance lanes touched).
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint all green; `go generate ./...` twice
  byte-identical; conformance green.
- Next: M4 parser consumes `Reader`.

## 2026-07-07 ‚Äî #11 xsd.QName ‚Äî Shipped

- Shipped (commit ef30b77): `xsd.QName` expanded-name value type (`xsd/qname.go`,
  `xsd/qname_test.go`). Struct of two strings (`Space`, `Local`) with a
  `String()` that renders Clark notation ("{ns}local"), no-namespace name as
  bare local, and the zero value as "" (absent/anonymous).
- Spec: Structures ¬ß2.2 (expanded name = namespace name + local name),
  ¬ß3.17.2.1 (QName value type). Zero-value-as-absent design noted against
  ¬ß2.2 key-null; no validation rule (this is the naming primitive).
- Decisions: (1) Exactly `QName` + `String()` exported (STYLE T5) ‚Äî no
  constructor, no Equal/IsAbsent helpers; comparability falls out of the
  two-string struct and is exercised by a map-key test. (2) `String()` uses
  plain concatenation, not strings.Builder, for a fixed three-part join. (3)
  Doc comment keeps "no-namespace present name" (key-null) textually distinct
  from "absent target namespace" (key-targetNS) per grounding.
- Ratchet: unchanged (pure leaf, stdlib-only, no conformance lanes touched).
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint all green (full `go test ./...` passes).
- Next: value.Backend / component-model indexes consume `xsd.QName` as map key.

## 2026-07-08 ‚Äî #12 regex.Translate ‚Äî Shipped

- Shipped (commits 064ad4d + repair 67c0c13): `regex` package
  (`regex/regex.go`, `regex/class.go`, `regex/classparse.go`,
  `regex/regex_test.go`) ‚Äî one recursive-descent translator core, two flavors
  (PRINCIPLES 10). `Translate(pattern, flavor, flags) (goRE, err)`: XSD
  pattern-facet flavor (implicit `\A(?:‚Ä¶)\z` anchor, literal `^`/`$`,
  non-capturing `(?:‚Ä¶)`, no flags, `.`‚Üí`[^\n\r]`) and F&O flavor (unanchored,
  real `^`/`$`, capturing groups, `i`/`s`/`m`‚Üí`(?i)(?s)(?m)`,
  `x`‚Üíwhitespace-strip preprocessing, `.`‚Üí`.`). Exported surface: `Flavor`,
  `FlavorXSD`, `FlavorFO`, `Translate` (STYLE T5). **Flavor redesigned
  (67c0c13)**: closed `uint8` enum with `iota+1` basis (invalid zero value is
  a caught bug); invalid Flavor or XSD-flavor with non-empty flags panic as
  caller-contract violations (programming errors), never return `*xsderr.Error`.
- Spec: Datatypes Appendix G (productions [64]‚Äì[98], ¬ßG.4.1 hyphen rules,
  ¬ßG.4.2.3 block-name normalization, ¬ßG.4.2.5 escape equivalences); F&O ¬ß7.6.1
  additions (anchors, capture, back-references, reluctant quantifiers) and
  ¬ß7.6.1.1 flags. Rule IDs: `src-pattern-value` (XSD translation failure),
  `err:FORX0002` (FO pattern), `err:FORX0001` (FO flags). Grounding:
  .agent/grounding-issue-12.md.
- Decisions: (1) Character-class algebra (subtraction `[a-z-[m]]`, negation,
  complement-valued escapes `\S`/`\D`/`\w`) has no RE2 form, so classes are
  parsed into an internal sorted-disjoint `runeSet` and emitted as flattened
  explicit ranges; standalone category escapes (`\p{L}`) and `\d`/`\w` pass
  through compactly. (2) `\w`=`[^\p{P}\p{Z}\p{C}]`, `\W`=`[\p{P}\p{Z}\p{C}]`
  ‚Äî the spec's full-range subtraction is exactly a complement, so no residual
  subtraction to represent. (3) Unicode block escapes (`\p{IsBasicLatin}`)
  translate via a curated hand-authored `unicodeBlocks` table (Go's stdlib
  exposes categories/scripts, not blocks; ranges from the Unicode DB, not the
  local specs). Unrecognized block/category is a HARD error, not the spec's
  ¬ßG.4.2.4 fail-open default ‚Äî goxsd8 forbids false accepts (PRINCIPLES 20).
  (4) `\i\I\c\C` (XML NameChar escapes) are out of scope, rejected as explicit
  "unsupported" errors (follow-up if suite case needs them). (5) Counted-repeat
  >1000 enforced at translation time (attributable to goxsd8, never silent
  truncation); not spec-mandated.
- xsderr: extended `tools/rulecat` to harvest F&O/XPath `err:FOXX0000` code
  family (54 codes) so `err:FORX0001/0002` are valid Rules (E2);
  `xsderr/catalog.go` regenerated (additive). The `regex/doc.go` and
  ARCHITECTURE.md wrongly claimed `m`/`x` are RE2-inexpressible ‚Äî corrected:
  RE2 supports `(?m)` and `x` is preprocessing, both honored per F&O ¬ß7.6.1.1.
- Warden verdict (ACCEPT WITH NITS): blocking [T1/T7] issue was `Flavor` as
  reassignable struct-wrapped var (illegal state). Repair (67c0c13) redesigned
  to closed `uint8` enum with invalid-zero-value panic. Invalid-Flavor and
  XSD-flags-with-FlavorXSD now panic (caller-contract violations) rather than
  return errors (STYLE E1: caller misuse ‚âÝ pattern error).
- Arbiter verdict (ACCEPT): full gate green (build/test/vet/lint/conformance);
  ratchet unchanged (no lanes touched); all 9 acceptance-criteria tests pass;
  style/determinism/spec-citation spot-check all clear; tests prove rejection of
  unsupported constructs (TestErrorsSurfaceNeverSilentlyAccepted asserts exact
  rule ID per case).

  specs still resolve to the cited editions and track in-place errata; only F&O

  later) and switched to wip/issue-13. Oracle grounded the session on Datatypes
  ¬ß4.2.1 rf-ordered (partial ordering), ¬ß2.2.2 equality + cvc-enumeration-valid
  (NaN identity vs order ‚Äî Identical/Ordered split), ¬ß3.3.18/¬ß3.3.19 QName/NOTATION
  context-dependent lexical mapping (why Mapping.Parse takes a Context), and
  dt-canonical-representation (Canonical optional, not required). Mason
  implemented value/value.go (`Value`, `Ordering`+4 consts, 8 capability
  interfaces: `Eq`/`Ordered`/`Identical`/`Lengthed`/`DigitCounted`/`Scaled`/
  `TimezoneAware`/`Canonical`) and value/backend.go (`Context`, `Mapping`,
  `Backend`, `Override`/overrideBackend, `LexicalFacet`/`ValueFacet`), rewrote
  value/doc.go referencing real symbols + preserving widest-space-rule prose
  verbatim, added value/backend_test.go (`TestOverride`) + value/example_test.go
  (`ExampleOverride`, go vet-checked, "back only xs:decimal with a money type"
  story from real xsd.QName). One nolint:revive on `ValueFacet` (justified
  stutter, spec-paired with `LexicalFacet`). Warden reviewed: APPROVE with two
  non-blocking doc nits (Parse/Override non-nil invariants), applied directly
  (commit c0502e6). Arbiter reviewed: ACCEPT. Full gate green (build/test/vet/
  lint), conformance suite unaffected (types-only change, ratchet correctly NOT
  run). Commit e7e4e8e.
- Spec: Datatypes ¬ß2.2.2 (equality), ¬ß3.3.18/¬ß3.3.19 (QName/NOTATION), ¬ß4.2
  (fundamental facets), ¬ß4.2.1 (rf-ordered), cvc-enumeration-valid (NaN), dt-
  canonical-representation.
- Ratchet: unchanged (types-only change, no conformance lanes touched).
- Decisions: (1) Eight interfaces + Value receiver methods model the capability
  algebra per ¬ß4.2 + ¬ß2.2.2 (Identical/Ordered distinction is spec-structural).
  (2) Mapping.Parse takes Context (QName/NOTATION are context-dependent per
  ¬ß3.3.18/¬ß3.3.19). (3) Canonical is optional (dt-canonical-representation:
  "Canonical representation is optional"); nil Mapping.Canonical is valid. (4)
  Override pattern: Backend + slice of Overrides; each Override.LexicalFacet
  wraps a fn rewriting type's lexical space, ValueFacet wraps a value-space
  capability to compose into final Backend. (5) Backend is the final contract
  surface (exported). LexicalFacet/ValueFacet are implementation types (unexported
  in value/doc.go), but exported in value/backend.go for testability + documentation.
- Next: issue #7 (value/backendtest design) can now proceed in a future session ‚Äî
  package `value` has its first real, compiling, tested code. The third-party-
  backend contract surface is ready for consumption by pattern facets and value-
  space derivation.
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint all green; conformance green; `go generate`
  unchanged (data-only, no code-gen dependency).

## 2026-07-09 ‚Äî issue #7 ‚Äî value/backendtest kit designed + boolean pipeline

- Shipped: `value/backendtest` skeleton (kit.go) ‚Äî the vector schema
  (`typeVectors`/`roundtrip`, unexported), `Option`/`Absent`, and `Run` over an
  internal `reporter` (the `*testing.T` subset, so the engine is fake-testable).
  New generator `tools/backendtestgen` reads `docs/specs/md/xmlschema11-2.md`
  and emits `gen_vectors.go` (wired via `//go:generate` in gen.go, go.mod tool
  block). Boolean vectors proven end to end: round-trip + invalid-rejection, two
  fakes (correct ‚Üí 0 failures, buggy ‚Üí >0), a public `Run` smoke test, and a
  `go vet`-checked `ExampleRun` showing `value.Override` composition. Design
  write-up in `.agent/design-issue-7.md` (posted as the issue comment).
- Spec: ¬ß3.3.2.2 f-booleanLexmap / f-booleanCanmap / nt-booleanRep;
  cvc-datatype-valid (¬ß4.1.4).
- Ratchet: unchanged (infrastructure; no conformance lanes wired).
- Decisions: (1) Schema unexported ‚Äî the kit's API is `Run`; the corpus is
  internal (STYLE T5). Exported surface = `Run`, `Option`, `Absent` only.
  (2) Vectors spec-derived by parsing the booleanRep production + lexical/
  canonical map clauses (PRINCIPLES 26); invalids are a mechanical near-miss
  sample of the nt-booleanRep complement. Generator fails loud on any parse
  surprise (STYLE S3). (3) `NarrowReject` schema slot reserved for the
  widest-space discipline; empty for boolean (primitive = widest). (4) `Run`
  coverage check scoped to types-with-vectors so `Absent` has a real consumer
  now; full 19-primitive coverage + capability/order/identity/widest-space
  checks deferred to the #27 concrete backend (documented gaps, not stubs).
  (5) `ExampleRun` pins `backendtest.Run` and shows the round-trip inline ‚Äî
  `Run` needs a `*testing.T` no Example can supply (known Go limitation).
- Next: file a follow-up issue (capability-coverage + order/identity +
  widest-space) blocked on #27 so the deferred doc.go bullets stay tracked.
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint all green; `go generate` byte-stable.

## 2026-07-10 ‚Äî #28 ‚Äî schema-closed constant sets (sealed typed constants)

- Shipped (commit 46ef298): new leaf file `xsd/closedsets.go` ‚Äî 7 sealed
  `uint8` enum types for the XSD 1.1 schema-closed scalar sets, matching the
  `builtin.Ordered` / `regex.Flavor` iota+1 idiom (invalid zero sentinel; no
  interface/marker-method sum since none of these carry a payload):
  - `AttributeUse` (¬ß3.2.2 lexical `use`: Optional/Prohibited/Required) ‚Äî
    explicitly the XML-representation attribute, NOT the Attribute Use
    component's `{required}` bool (a separate fact deferred to a later issue).
  - `ContentTypeVariety` (¬ß3.4.1: Empty/Simple/ElementOnly‚Üí"element-only"/Mixed).
  - `OpenContentMode` (¬ß3.4.1 component `{mode}`: Interleave/Suffix ‚Äî
    deliberately 2-valued; XML-lexical `mode="none"` (¬ß3.4.2.3) means the Open
    Content component is absent, not a third constant, keeping "present but
    mode=none" unrepresentable).
  - `Compositor` (¬ß3.8.1: All/Choice/Sequence).
  - `DerivationMethod` (shared 5-token vocabulary across ¬ß3.3.1/¬ß3.4.1/
    xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß4.1.1: Extension/Restriction/Substitution/List/Union ‚Äî
    documented as NOT asserting all 5 are legal in every consuming context;
    per-property subset validation deferred to future issues with real
    consumers).
  - `ProcessContents` (¬ß3.10.1: Skip/Strict/Lax).
  - `ValueConstraintKind` (¬ß3.2.1/¬ß3.3.1/¬ß3.5.1: Default/Fixed ‚Äî named "Kind"
    not "Variety" to avoid colliding with the unrelated simple-type variety
    term of art).
  Every `String()` is a switch (never a map ‚Äî D3), non-panicking default
  (`"AttributeUse(0)"`-style diagnostic). No constructors, no reverse
  `Parse<T>(string)` (no consumer yet, T5/T8). All constants type-prefixed to
  avoid future namespace collisions. Pure leaf: imports only `strconv`.
- Scoped OUT deliberately: `Form` (qualified/unqualified) dropped from the
  original 8-item issue scope ‚Äî the oracle's grounding found there is no
  `{form}` schema-component property anywhere in the spec; `form` is purely an
  XML-representation attribute fully consumed into `{target namespace}` at
  parse time with zero residual component presence, so landing it here would be
  an unjustified/unconsumed export (T5/T8). Deferred to whichever future
  parser/mapping-rules issue actually needs it.
- Spec: ¬ß3.2.1/¬ß3.2.2 (attribute use / value constraint), ¬ß3.3.1 (simple-type
  {final}), ¬ß3.4.1/¬ß3.4.2.3 (content type variety, open content {mode}),
  ¬ß3.5.1 (attribute value constraint), ¬ß3.8.1 (compositor), ¬ß3.10.1 (wildcard
  process contents), xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß4.1.1 (derivation-method vocabulary).
- Process: oracle grounding found the issue's original 8-item premise imprecise
  in 4 of 8 spots ‚Äî `AttributeUse` conflated the lexical `use` attribute with
  the component `{required}` bool; `OpenContentMode` conflated the 3-valued
  XML-lexical set with the 2-valued component property; `DerivationMethod`
  conflated FOUR differently-sized consuming sets under one label; `Form` isn't
  a component property at all. Warden pre-flight (before code) resolved all
  four: ship AttributeUse as the lexical set only, ship OpenContentMode
  2-valued only, ship DerivationMethod as one shared unconstrained vocabulary
  with per-site validation deferred, and scope Form out entirely. Mason
  implemented exactly to the warden spec.
- Tests: `xsd/closedsets_test.go` ‚Äî one table test per type, each constant's
  exact spec-token `String()` output plus a zero-value and an out-of-range (99)
  case exercising the non-panicking default branch.
- Verdicts: Warden pre-flight (posted on #28) APPROVED the design with the four
  scoping decisions above plus naming/shape rulings (scalar uint8 not interface
  sum; switch not map for String(); type-prefixed constant names;
  ValueConstraintKind not ‚Ä¶Variety). Arbiter ACCEPT at 46ef298, FINDINGS none ‚Äî
  verified STYLE compliance, spot-checked spec citations against docs/specs/md
  (confirmed "element-only" is genuinely hyphenated, confirmed OpenContentMode's
  2-valued component property vs 3-valued XML-lexical distinction), confirmed
  Form was not sneaked in, confirmed test integrity.
- Gate: go build/test/vet ./... green; golangci-lint 0 issues; conformance
  (TestConformance) pass.
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî leaf types touch no conformance lanes; confirmed
  `git diff origin/main -- conformance/testdata/expectations/` empty both before
  and after the arbiter's `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` run.
- Landing: cleared by arbiter at 46ef298; lands via PR squash-merged as one
  commit (Closes #28), then the cartographer's post-land unblock + follow-up
  harvest pass.
- Next: several open `ready` issues (#33 SimpleType, #34 namespace-constraint/
  Wildcard allowance, #35 Assertion, #36 identity-constraints, #29 particle
  occurrence range, #30 Notation/Annotation, #38 doc/flag cleanup, #39 XSD
  namespace constants) coordinate with #28's enum conventions ‚Äî none blocked on
  #28 specifically (all "Depends on: none"), but #33/#34/#35/#36 mention
  matching #28's constant-naming conventions, now established as: type-prefixed
  constants, scalar uint8 not interface sum for payload-free closed sets,
  switch-based String(). Two deferred/unshipped items for the cartographer's
  post-land harvest pass (do NOT self-file): (1) the `Form` scope-out ‚Äî
  deferred to the future parser/mapping-rules issue that actually consumes
  `form`; (2) the `DerivationMethod` per-property subset validation gap ‚Äî

## 2026-07-10 ‚Äî #29 particle occurrence range ‚Äî shipped

- Shipped: `xsd.Occurs` value type ‚Äî the particle {min occurs}/{max occurs}
  range (Structures ¬ß3.9.1) with an unbounded max, illegal states
  unrepresentable. New file `xsd/occurs.go` + `xsd/occurs_test.go`.
- Exported surface: `Occurs` struct (unexported fields min/max); constructors
  `NewOccurs(min, max int) (Occurs, error)` (bounded) and
  `NewUnboundedOccurs(min int) (Occurs, error)`; methods `Min() int`,
  `IsUnbounded() bool`, `Max() (int, bool)` (ok-idiom, no exported sentinel),
  `Permits(n int) bool`, `String() string`.
- Design: unbounded encoded as a private `unboundedMax = -1` sentinel in the
  single `max` field (STYLE D3 one-fact-one-encoding; T1 ‚Äî "unbounded yet
  bounded to N" unrepresentable). Ok-idiom Max chosen over an exported sentinel
  so no caller handles a magic maxOccurs literal. Constructors reject negative
  min, negative bounded max, and bounded max < min, all as `*xsderr.Error`
  under rule `p-props-correct`. Zero value is the legal vacuous 0..0 particle
  (¬ß3.9.2 admits maxOccurs 0), documented as such ‚Äî not an absent/invalid
  marker. String renders "1" / "2..5" / "1..unbounded" (token spelled exactly).
- Spec: p-props-correct (Particle Correct ¬ß3.9.6.1) clause 1 (property value
  spaces: nonNegativeInteger min, allNNI max) + clause 2.1 (min not greater
  than numeric max). Clause 2 does not fire when max is unbounded ‚Äî no
  upper-bound check, matching the constructor split.
- Catalog: `p-props-correct` is a genuine spec anchor but an irregular rule ID
  (no cvc-/cos-/src-/sic- prefix), so it was absent from the generated
  catalog. Added it to `tools/rulecat`'s `irregularRules` and regenerated
  `xsderr/catalog.go` via `go generate ./...` (generator + output committed
  together, PRINCIPLES 26/27) ‚Äî not hand-typed.
- Gate: go build/test/vet ./... green; golangci-lint 0 issues; conformance
  (TestConformance) pass.
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî pure leaf value type, touches no conformance lanes.
- Next: arbiter review, then land via PR (Closes #29).

## 2026-07-10 ‚Äî issue #33 ‚Äî xsd SimpleType definition component (datatypes-facing subset)

- Shipped (commit e0e647e): `xsd/simpletype.go` ‚Äî `Variety` sealed sum (`Atomic{Primitive
  *SimpleType}`, `List{Item *SimpleType}`, `Union{Members []*SimpleType}`;
  exported read-only fields, post-resolution live pointers, distinct from
  `builtin.Variety` per cross-referenced godoc); `FacetKind` 14-member sealed
  enum (¬ß4.3.1‚Äì4.3.14) with verbatim-token `String()` and derived `HasFixed()`
  (false only for pattern/enumeration/assertions); `Facet` (kind + values +
  fixed) with `NewFacet` normalizing `fixed` away when `!HasFixed()` (T1) and
  house `Fixed() (bool, bool)` accessor; `SimpleType` (`*SimpleType`, pointer
  identity) + `NewSimpleType` rejecting substitution in `{final}` and duplicate
  facet kinds (both `st-props-correct`), with `Name/Variety/Base/
  IsAnySimpleType/IsPrimitive/OwnFacets/EffectiveFacets/Final` accessors.
  `EffectiveFacets` computes `{facets}` on demand via ¬ß3.16.6.4 overlay (D3, no
  cache), deterministic base-to-derived order. Unexported `anySimpleType`/
  `anyAtomicType` anchors constructed as genuine `*SimpleType` singletons so the
  nil `Base()`/`Variety()`/`Primitive` contracts are exercised. Local
  `xsdNamespace` constant pending #39.
- Generator: added `st-props-correct` to `tools/rulecat` `irregularRules` (same
  family as `sch-/p-/n-/an-props-correct`), regenerated `xsderr/catalog.go` ‚Äî
  exactly one new sorted entry; `IsValidRule("st-props-correct")` now true.
- Tests: `xsd/simpletype_test.go` ‚Äî NewFacet fixed-normalization + value
  non-aliasing, FacetKind String/HasFixed, NewSimpleType substitution + dup-kind
  rejection, anchor nil-contract, IsPrimitive across anchor/primitive/derived,
  Own vs Effective facets on a 3-level chain (override masking + survival +
  order).
- Spec: st-props-correct (¬ß3.16.6.1 cl.4/5), variety/facets ¬ß3.16.1, ¬ß4.3,
  ¬ß2.4.2, ¬ß3.16.6.4.
- Verdicts: Warden pre-flight (posted on #33 before code) REVISE ‚Äî six rulings,
  all folded in before implementation: (1) `Variety` APPROVE as a sealed sum
  distinct from `builtin.Variety` (post-resolution live `*SimpleType` pointers
  + `Union`; unifying would invert the `builtin‚Üíxsd` dependency and break D4);
  (2) `Facet` {fixed} REVISE ‚Äî a "meaningful only when HasFixed()" bool is the
  T1 trap the grounding flagged, so `NewFacet` normalizes it away when
  `!HasFixed()` and the accessor is the house `Fixed() (fixed, ok bool)` idiom
  (NOT 14 per-kind structs, a T4 smell); (3) `Base()==nil` REVISE ‚Äî add derived
  `IsAnySimpleType()` so callers never infer identity from nil-ness; (4) RULING
  build the `anySimpleType`/`anyAtomicType` anchors HERE as unexported
  `*SimpleType` singletons (the only values where nil variety/base/Primitive is
  legal ‚Äî makes those contracts testable, T5, and forecloses a second
  anySimpleType); (5) OwnFacets/EffectiveFacets APPROVE ‚Äî `EffectiveFacets`
  godoc must state it IS the ¬ß3.16.1 {facets} property and return a
  deterministic doc-order slice (D2) despite the spec set-modeling; (6) {final}
  REVISE ‚Äî reuse `xsd.DerivationMethod` (no new type), reject `substitution`,
  and onboard `st-props-correct` to `tools/rulecat` `irregularRules` +
  regenerate the catalog BEFORE the constructor cites it. Warden diff-review
  APPROVE (no blockers), two non-blocking advisory notes: the variety-branch
  exported fields `Atomic.Primitive`/`List.Item`/`Union.Members` rely on
  "read-only by convention" ‚Äî a mild T1 smell accepted within the sealed-sum
  idiom + D4 phased construction (no illegal state is representable within a
  single branch); and `Atomic.Primitive` is technically derivable from the base
  chain but is modeled as the spec's first-class variety-specific property
  (with `IsPrimitive()` correctly derived, not stored ‚Äî not a D3 violation).
  Arbiter ACCEPT at e0e647e, FINDINGS none blocking; independently echoed both
  advisory notes. Charged `st-props-correct`'s two construction-time rejections
  to clause 1 (illegal `{final}` token ‚Üí property tableau) and clause 4
  (duplicate own-facet kind); verified the overlay empirically ‚Äî reverting the
  same-kind drop in `overlayFacet` fails `TestOwnVsEffectiveFacets`, so the
  3-level chain test genuinely asserts override-masking + survival + order, not
  mere presence. Verdicts posted on issue #33.
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî pure leaf, no conformance lanes; ratchet-write mode
  (`GOXSD_RATCHET=1`) deliberately not run since this adds no
  conformance-tested behavior. Catalog regen byte-clean (`xsderr/catalog.go`
  regenerates identically, one new sorted entry `st-props-correct`).
- Gate: build/test/vet green, golangci-lint 0 issues, `go generate` byte-clean.
- Next: land via PR squash-merged as one commit (Closes #33), then the
  cartographer's post-land unblock + follow-up harvest pass. Follow-ups for
  that pass to file or explicitly dismiss (do NOT self-file):
  (1) cross-type variety/base shape validation ‚Äî this leaf charges only
  st-props-correct clause 1 + clause 4; the per-variety {base}/{item}/{member}
  shape constraints (¬ß3.16.1/¬ß4.1.1: atomic base atomic, list item
  atomic-or-union-of-atomics, union members simple types), st-props-correct
  clauses 2/3/5, and `cos-st-restricts` are deferred to a later phase with a
  real producer/consumer (phased construction D4). The advisory note on the
  read-only-by-convention variety fields feeds this future cross-type issue.
  (2) the #14 deferred-work pointer (comment on #33) is now unblocked by this
  concrete facet model: `builtin/strict` pattern-facet wiring (regex XSD
  flavor, #12) + value-facet constructors (bounds / totalDigits+fractionDigits
  / length / enumeration) + widest-space / `*-valid-restriction` certification
  should be carved one layer above `xsd`.
  (3) LEAK ‚Äî the libuser provenance criterion (comment on #33, 2026-07-09,
  posted as body-level "not optional / load-bearing for #14") asked the
  effective-facets view to expose each facet's declaring-type `xsd.QName`, so
  `value`'s widest-space rule can compare an inherited facet in the space of
  the type that DECLARES it. `EffectiveFacets` shipped as a bare `[]Facet` with
  provenance flattened away (the warden pre-flight approved that shape without
  reconciling it against the criterion). Unshipped ‚Äî needs a tracking issue or
  an explicit dismissal.
- Repair (pre-landing): the item-3 provenance LEAK was caught before landing
  and fixed ‚Äî `EffectiveFacets` now returns `[]EffectiveFacet`, each pairing the
  `Facet` with its declaring type's `xsd.QName` (`Facet()`/`Declaring()`
  accessors; zero QName for an anonymous ancestor), honoring the libuser
  body-level criterion (comment on #33, 2026-07-09) so `value`'s widest-space
  rule can compare an inherited facet in its declaring type's space. `OwnFacets`
  unchanged. Test asserts declaring provenance across the 3-level chain plus the
  anonymous-ancestor zero-QName case.

## 2026-07-10 ‚Äî issue #15 ‚Äî builtin.Seed composition + first datatypes ratchet lane (M3)

- Shipped `builtin/seed.go`: `Seed(b value.Backend) ([]*xsd.SimpleType, error)`
  composes the generated `Types` table with a backend into ready
  `*xsd.SimpleType` components. Returns `len(Types)+1` components,
  deterministic: **xs:anySimpleType prepended, then Types in order**.
  anySimpleType is synthesized once (nil variety/base) and reused as
  xs:anyAtomicType's base, so the one-node-per-identity rule holds
  (pointer identity is load-bearing per `xsd.SimpleType`). Base chain wired
  via recursive memoized build (Types is not base-before-derived ‚Äî anyAtomicType
  is row 48, referenced by rows 1‚Äì19). Derived atomics get their {primitive
  type definition} ancestor pointer; primitives + anyAtomicType carry nil
  (a primitive's self-reference is inexpressible through `xsd.NewSimpleType`,
  documented as a bounded gap). Own facets = value-bearing spec defaults from
  the row (cos-applicable-facets ¬ß4.1.5); applicable-but-unset facets are not
  attached. precisionDecimal's maxScale/minScale carry no default and have no
  `xsd.FacetKind`, so they never reach the translator.
- `MissingPrimitivesError`: plain typed Go error (NOT xsderr ‚Äî a precondition
  fault on Seed's `b` arg, no cvc-*/cos-* rule per oracle grounding), collects
  ALL unmapped primitives in Types order, never empty (built only inside
  `len(missing) > 0`), `errors.As`-detectable. Precondition scans the 20
  primitive rows (`TypeSpec.IsPrimitive()` = Base=="anyAtomicType", includes
  precisionDecimal-by-project-policy, excludes anyAtomicType's own row).
  nil-slice on any error (no partial).
- `builtin/doc.go` line 68 fixed: anySimpleType now comes FROM Seed's slice;
  only xs:anyType (complex, out of scope) stays a parser-structural concern.
  Seeding section rewritten to match the shipped contract.
- Godoc obligations (libuser criteria) met: order, idempotency/purity,
  error shape + `errors.As`, anyType/anySimpleType membership. Runnable
  `ExampleSeed` (consumption idiom ‚Üí `map[QName]*SimpleType` symbol table) and
  `ExampleSeed_missingPrimitive` (`errors.As` on an empty stub backend).
  README library Quickstart now names `Seed` as the required first step.
- Conformance `datatypes` lane activated (`conformance/datatypes.go`, edits only
  the `datatypes` entry of `defaultLanes` ‚Äî the #6 seam untouched). Cohort:
  the MS `msData/datatypes/{boolean,decimal,string}NNN.xml` LEXICAL instances ‚Äî
  elements of UNRESTRICTED builtins, so validity == primitive lexical-space
  membership == `value.Mapping.Parse`. 49 cases; the executor is genuine (real
  docs, real Parse, both polarities decided for the right reason: boolean
  rejects True/+1/""; decimal rejects e/1E4/INF/NaN/13.1513.561/ABCDEF).
  NIST/MS-Facets corpora were investigated and rejected (facet-invalid
  instances stay lexically valid ‚Üí Parse-blind; a facet engine is later).
  Test-only fallback backend maps the 17 primitives strict lacks so
  `builtin.Seed`'s precondition is met (`value.Override(fallback, strict.New())`);
  those mappings are never exercised (selector claims only decimal/boolean/
  string). Read-only run: 49 cases claimed, no regression; 48 genuine pass +
  1 honest gap (boolean018, a list-of-boolean+enumeration ‚Äî its type resolves
  to user-defined `myList`, not a seeded primitive, so honestly recorded Fail,
  proving the executor is not fake-always-pass).
- Spec: cos-applicable-facets (¬ß4.1.5); primitives ¬ß3.3 / ¬ß3.16.7.4 (prose
  obligation, no rule ID ‚Äî grounding); precisionDecimal always-on by project
  policy (xsd-precisionDecimal.md).
- Gate: build + `go test ./...` + vet + `golangci-lint run` (0 issues) all green.
  Ratchet NOT run (arbiter-only); the first `datatypes.txt` lands via the
  arbiter's `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` separately.

## 2026-07-10 ‚Äî issue #15 ‚Äî warden repair round (primitive identity)

- Warden REJECTED `a3d69b6` (two must-fix, one root cause): Seed emitted
  `Atomic{Primitive: nil}` for all 20 primitives (contradicts `xsd.Atomic`'s
  contract ‚Äî nil means "IS xs:anyAtomicType"), and `IsPrimitive()` returned
  false for every Seed-produced primitive (Seed synthesized its own
  anySimpleType/anyAtomicType, so pointer identity failed against xsd's private
  singletons).
- `xsd/simpletype.go`: added `NewPrimitiveType(loc, name, ownFacets, final)` ‚Äî
  a self-wiring constructor that fixes {base type definition} to the canonical
  xs:anyAtomicType and wires `Atomic{Primitive: t}` on the node it allocates,
  inside the constructor before it escapes (immutable to external callers,
  ¬ß3.16.1 "a primitive's {primitive type definition} is that datatype itself").
  Added `AnySimpleType()`/`AnyAtomicType()` accessors returning the package
  singletons (STYLE-T5-justified: Seed is the first real consumer, warden
  blessed). Extracted shared `checkSTProps`/`setOwnFacetsFinal` so
  NewSimpleType and NewPrimitiveType validate/copy identically.
- `builtin/seed.go`: roots the graph on `xsd.AnySimpleType()`/`AnyAtomicType()`
  (no more duplicate synthesis) and builds the 20 primitive rows through
  `xsd.NewPrimitiveType`. Single pointer identity now spans the whole graph;
  `IsPrimitive()` is true for every Seed primitive; a primitive's
  {primitive type definition} self-references. Godoc (Seed + doc.go) reconciled:
  primitives self-reference, only xs:anyAtomicType carries nil; Purity note now
  states the two anchors are shared immutable singletons.
- `conformance/datatypes.go`: `Seed` error now check-and-panics (programming
  error ‚Äî the composed backend is complete by construction) instead of dropping.
- Tests: new `TestSeedPrimitivesReportIsPrimitive` (every primitive
  `IsPrimitive()`==true, base is canonical anchor, self-referential Primitive;
  the two special types are not primitive); updated
  `TestSeedBaseChainAndPrimitivePointer` (decimal.Primitive == decimal) and
  `TestSeedIdempotentIndependentGraphs` (anchors shared, all other nodes
  independent).
- Spec: st-props-correct (¬ß3.16.6.1); ¬ß3.16.1 (primitive {primitive type
  definition}); ¬ß4.1.6 (anyAtomicType). Ratchet: unchanged.
- Gate: build + `go test ./...` + vet + `golangci-lint run` (0 issues) + read-
  only conformance all green.

- Ratchet: `datatypes` 0 ‚Üí 49 (48 pass / 1 fail) ‚Äî first lane populated.
- Next: this closes the M3 "first datatypes lane" deliverable. #45 (pattern +
  value-facet pipeline stages) is the natural next step to widen the lane beyond
  the 49-case unrestricted-literal cohort into restricted/derived types.

  design on #35 ‚Äî implemented verbatim, no redesign.

  on package xpath), carries the ALREADY-RESOLVED {default namespace} through
  the ¬ß3.13.2 xpathDefaultNamespace chain (the tree-walk is the parser's job),
  and models {namespace bindings} as a document-order slice (STYLE D2).
  {default namespace} / {base URI} use the pointer-present / nil-absent
  discipline (mirrors AppInfo {source}) so "" stays a legal present anyURI.

  back TypeAlternative.Test() (Optional) and identity-constraint selector/
  fields in later issues (¬ß3.13.2 defines the record once, all mappings
  reuse it), and serves simple-type assertions via the ¬ß4.3.13 facet.
- No rejectable state at this layer ‚Üí constructors return no error (mirrors
  NewAnnotation). Tests bite via mutation: defensive-copy in AND out, nil-on-
  empty, and the present-empty-string vs absent distinction.
- Spec: ¬ß3.13.1 (Assertion, XPath Expression, Namespace Binding), ¬ß3.13.2
  (default-namespace resolution), ¬ß4.3.13 (assertions facet reuse).

- Shipped: builtin/strict/facets.go + facets_test.go ‚Äî the pattern (lexical)
  and value (enumeration/bounds/digits/length) facet pipeline stages running
  after the whiteSpace stage over the decimal/boolean/string cohort. New
  driving fn checkAgainstType wires the fixed sequence whiteSpace ‚Üí pattern ‚Üí
  lexical mapping ‚Üí value facets; compile() builds []value.LexicalFacet /
  []value.ValueFacet from EffectiveFacets and drives them polymorphically
  (justifying the pre-declared pipeline-stage interfaces). All symbols
  unexported ‚Äî go doc shows zero new exported names (Surface: none, per warden
  pre-flight).
- Widest-space rule (st-restrict-facets ¬ß3.16.6.4) proven, not just wired:
  declaringMapping walks from the leaf to the facet's DECLARING type, then to
  its nearest mapped ancestor. Test builds decimalPrim ‚Üê lvl1{urn:test,
  maxInclusive=100} ‚Üê leaf{urn:test}; the effective facet's Declaring() is
  lvl1 (NOT xsdNS-mapped), forcing the walk lvl1 ‚Üí decimalPrim to find the
  mapping ‚Äî "150" rejected, "50" accepted.
- Verdicts: Arbiter ACCEPT at 5471932.
- Spec: cvc-pattern-valid, cvc-enumeration-valid, cvc-{max,min}{In,Ex}clusive-
  valid, cvc-{total,fraction}Digits-valid, cvc-{,min,max}Length-valid,
  st-restrict-facets. Per-facet rule IDs cited on every xsderr.Error (never
  the cvc-facet-valid umbrella).
- Decisions/deviations: (1) whiteSpace mode resolved from st's PRIMITIVE
  ancestor via the existing whiteSpaceOf/builtin.Types machinery (fixed at the
  primitive for this cohort), so hand-built derived nodes need no whiteSpace
  facet ‚Äî smallest correct extension (STYLE D3). (2) Pattern test uses
  "[a-z]+" not "^[a-z]+$": regex.FlavorXSD anchors the whole literal and treats
  ^/$ as literal characters. (3) enumMatch unions value.Eq with value.Identical
  (spec: "equal OR identical"). (4) Bounds Incomparable / missing capability =
  panic (internal-consistency bug, cos-applicable-facets not enforced upstream),
  never a spec rejection. (5) regex constant is regex.FlavorXSD (issue text said
  regex.XSD). No xsd/value source touched.
- Ratchet: unchanged (no new conformance lanes wired).
- Gate: build/test/vet all green; golangci-lint 0 issues (converted trailing
  panics to default: cases for the exhaustive linter, default-signifies-
  exhaustive is on); conformance green.

## 2026-07-11 ‚Äî issue #48 ‚Äî xsd.ValueConstraint ({value constraint} holder)

- Shipped (commit 3bcd3c0): new leaf files `xsd/valueconstraint.go` +
  `xsd/valueconstraint_test.go` (+87 lines, two new files, no existing files
  touched) ‚Äî `ValueConstraint` pairs the already-exported
  `xsd.ValueConstraintKind` (default/fixed, from #28) with the {value
  constraint} record's {lexical form} field (the normalized lexical string).
  Immutable struct, validating constructor `NewValueConstraint(kind,
  lexicalForm)`, value-receiver accessors `Kind() ValueConstraintKind` and
  `LexicalForm() string`.
- Exported surface added: `ValueConstraint`, `NewValueConstraint`, `Kind()`,
  `LexicalForm()`. No `Fixed() bool` predicate (STYLE D3 ‚Äî derivable from
  `Kind()`).
- Deliberately omits the record's third field, {value} (the parsed ¬∑actual
  value¬∑): `xsd` is a pure leaf (imports only `xsderr` + stdlib per doc.go)
  and cannot import `value`, and which type's mapping governs parsing is a
  decision only a value-aware consumer can make. The godoc names the future M4
  element/attribute/attribute-use declaration consumers as the T8
  justification for landing a leaf ahead of its consumer.
- Spec: Structures ¬ß3.2.1 vc_a (attribute declaration), ¬ß3.3.1 vc_e (element
  declaration), ¬ß3.5.1 vc_au (attribute use) ‚Äî the three sites of the
  three-field Value Constraint record ({variety}/{value}/{lexical form}), with
  "default"/"fixed" as verbatim {variety} tokens.
- Decisions: (1) accessor named `LexicalForm()`, NOT the issue body's original
  `Value()` sketch ‚Äî {value} in spec terms is the parsed actual value this
  holder deliberately does not carry, so `Value()` would have been a consumer
  trap (warden pre-flight ACCEPT-WITH-CHANGES). (2) Zero value is NOT
  meaningful (invalid {variety}) ‚Äî documented in explicit contrast with
  QName's "zero means absent" convention, per warden.
- Verdicts: oracle grounding (quoted the three-field record verbatim at
  vc_a/vc_e/vc_au, confirmed the {value}-vs-{lexical form} actual-vs-normalized
  distinction) ‚Üí warden pre-flight (ACCEPT-WITH-CHANGES: Value‚ÜíLexicalForm,
  zero-value + T8-consumer doc additions) ‚Üí mason implementation ‚Üí arbiter
  (ACCEPT ‚Äî full gate green, conformance no-op confirmed). All posted on issue
  #48.
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî pure structural xsd leaf, no parser/validator wiring
  yet. Arbiter confirmed the committed `datatypes.txt` baseline byte-identical.
- Surprise: the arbiter's `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` run incidentally materialized 5
  untracked lane-baseline artifacts (schema/instance/xpath/json/ber.txt) that
  reproduce on main and are unrelated to this diff; arbiter removed them to
  leave the tree clean. Tracked separately as issue #65.
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint/conformance all green (per arbiter).
- Next: the M4 declaration components consume `ValueConstraint`; the oracle
  flagged a probable future local-attribute-declaration / AttributeUse issue as
  the first such consumer.

## 2026-07-11 ‚Äî issue #57 ‚Äî datatypes lane widened to the MS Facets cohort

- Shipped: `conformance/datatypes.go` widened beyond the 49-case lexical
  cohort to also claim the MS `Facets/{string,decimal}/*.xml` instance cases
  and decide them through the REAL facet pipeline. Companion change: exported
  `builtin/strict`'s facet-pipeline entry point `checkAgainstType` verbatim as
  `strict.ValidateLexical` (pure visibility rename + T7 panic-precondition
  godoc; identical body/signature). (this session's commit).
- Surface: one exported symbol added ‚Äî `strict.ValidateLexical`. Warden gave an
  advisory-APPROVE pre-flight (right seam; do not relocate) with three diff
  conditions, all satisfied: (T7) godoc documents the panic on inapplicable
  facet / no primitive ancestor; (T1) the conformance executor OWNS
  applicability ‚Äî it attaches only facets `builtin.TypeSpec.Applies` confirms
  for the base primitive (cos-applicable-facets ¬ß4.1.5), so the panic path is
  never reached and inapplicable/odd-shape cases are declined (Fail gap), not
  crashed; (T4) pure visibility change in strict, in-package test call sites
  renamed, no forked normalization ‚Äî the facet path lets ValidateLexical's
  whiteSpace stage normalize (existing `normalizeWhiteSpace` stays lexical-only,
  one path each).
- Spec rules wired via the pipeline: cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4,
  cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4, cvc-enumeration-valid ¬ß4.3.5.4,
  cvc-min/maxInclusive/Exclusive-valid ¬ß4.3.7‚Äì4.3.10, cvc-totalDigits-valid
  ¬ß4.3.11.3, cvc-length/minLength/maxLength-valid ¬ß4.3.1.3‚Äì4.3.3.3;
  applicability gate cos-applicable-facets ¬ß4.1.5.
- Cohort result (DIAG-measured, pre-arbiter): 41 Facets cases claimed, 39
  decided correctly through the pipeline (both polarities; facet-invalid-but-
  lexically-valid instances now correctly rejected ‚Äî the class #15 deferred), 2
  declined as honest gaps (an attribute-carried value with no xsi schema
  location; a list-variety namespaced case). boolean018 unchanged (Fail): still
  a non-seeded list type, out of reach until list variety lands.
- Ratchet: datatypes lane expected to move 48/1 ‚Üí 87/3 (strict increase, nothing
  pass‚Üífail). NOT run here (arbiter-only); read-only
  `go test ./conformance -run TestConformance` green with 0 regressed. The other
  lanes' expectation files are absent (empty lanes), so the Facets cases moving
  out of the inert `instance` lane produce no Vanished cases.
- Gate: build/test/vet green; golangci-lint 0 issues.
- Next: arbiter judge + ratchet; follow-ups for boolean/list-variety Facets and
  the NIST corpus once their backends exist.
- Post-land pass (2026-07-11): unblock scan a no-op (no `blocked` issue depends
  on #57). NIST corpus + narrower-primitive + list/union lane widening filed as
  **#75** (`blocked` on #60 + later primitive/variety cohorts); warden's

  separate tracker (rides in the lane as a recorded `fail` per the #57/#15

  golangci-lint 0 issues). Ratchet run (`GOXSD_RATCHET=1`) confirmed a strict
  upward move on the datatypes lane: 48/1 ‚Üí 87/3 (41 new Facets cases, 0

  a decline yields Fail() unconditionally, and the expectation records "pass"

  both polarities. Panic-unreachability re-verified independently: the leaf is
  built with a real primitive ancestor (the seeded base) and buildOwnFacets

## 2026-07-12 ‚Äî #59 ‚Äî STYLE D3: drop redundant rule field from strict facets

- Shipped (commit dfaf065, "builtin/strict: drop redundant rule field from
  bound/digits/lengthFacet (#59)"): removed the `rule xsderr.Rule` field from
  `boundFacet`, `digitsFacet`, and `lengthFacet` in `builtin/strict/facets.go`.
  The field was pure derived state ‚Äî always `boundRule(kind)` / `digitsRule(kind)`
  / `lengthRule(kind)` for the facet's own kind ‚Äî so it duplicated a fact already
  encoded by the mapper. Every read site now calls the mapper directly at use
  instead of caching the result on the struct.
- Spec: n/a (style-only refactor; no rule behavior changed ‚Äî the same
  cvc-*-valid rule IDs still map from the same facet kinds).
- Ratchet: unchanged (no conformance behavior touched; expectations/ untouched).
- Decisions: one fact, one encoding (STYLE D3) ‚Äî a field derivable from the
  facet kind via an existing mapper is redundant state, not a cache (no measured
  hot path justifies it). No exported-surface change, no spec-behavior change.
- Provenance: advisory [D3] finding first flagged by the arbiter on #45's ACCEPT
  verdict; filed as its own issue (#59) rather than folded into #57 since it was
  outside #57's scope.
- Verdicts: Arbiter ACCEPTED with no findings ‚Äî full gate green
  (build/test/vet/golangci-lint 0 issues, conformance), ratchet unchanged.
- Next: n/a ‚Äî self-contained cleanup; the follow-up ledger for #45's advisory
  notes is now clear on the [D3] item.

## 2026-07-12 ‚Äî #60 ‚Äî builtin/strict: xs:float + xs:double primitive mappings (IEEE partial order)

- Shipped: `builtin/strict/float.go` ‚Äî spec-exact `value.Mapping`s for xs:float
  (IEEE binary32, Go `float32`) and xs:double (binary64, `float64`), the next
  primitive cohort after decimal/boolean/string. `strict.New()` now maps 5 of
  the 20 primitives; dispatch + `New` godoc + `doc.go` coverage updated.
  Each value is `value.Ordered` (PARTIAL order), `value.Eq`, `value.Identical`,
  `value.Canonical` ‚Äî and deliberately none of Lengthed/DigitCounted/Scaled
  (cos-applicable-facets ¬ß4.1.5). Shared lexical/canonical/compare logic lives in
  free functions on `float64`; the two named types keep value-space identity so a
  float-vs-double comparison is Incomparable.
- Spec: floatLexicalMap/doubleLexicalMap (f-floatLexmap/f-doubleLexmap, ¬ß3.3.4.2/
  ¬ß3.3.5.2); value space IEEE 754 (¬ß3.3.4/¬ß3.3.5); partial order with NaN
  incomparable (¬ß3.3.4.3/¬ß3.3.5.3, rf-ordered); equality vs identity carve-out
  (¬ß2.2.2: NaN‚âÝNaN but identical to itself, +0=‚àí0 but not identical);
  scientificCanonicalMap/specialRepCanonicalMap (f-sciCanFragMap/f-specValCanMap,
  Appendix E); invalid-lexical ‚Üí cvc-datatype-valid (¬ß4.1.4). Grounded by the
  oracle (issue #60 GROUNDING comment); the stricter special sub-grammar
  (nt-numSpecReps: bare `NaN` only, `+INF` the only signed special) is honored ‚Äî
  `+NaN`/`-NaN` are rejected.
- Facet pipeline: `builtin/strict/facets.go` `boundFacet.CheckValue` no longer
  PANICS on a `value.Incomparable` comparison ‚Äî it now REJECTS (excludes from the
  restricted value space, ¬ß3.3.4.3/¬ß3.3.5.3 Note). float/double is the first
  cohort with a genuine partial order, so this is the first primitive that
  actually reaches that branch (#45 decision 4 could only panic on it for the
  totally-ordered decimal cohort). Proven both directions in
  `TestBoundFacetNaNExcluded` (NaN instance vs numeric bound; NaN bound ‚Üí empty
  space).
- Data: `value/backendtest/gen_vectors.go` regenerated via extended
  `tools/backendtestgen` (parseFloating derives float/double vectors from the
  spec: special literals from nt-numSpecReps, extracted+verified lexical regex,
  representative numerals canonicalised by an independent scientificCanonicalMap
  oracle, regex-verified near-miss invalids). Generator tests pin the corpus
  (TestFloatVectors/TestDoubleVectors, TestApplicableFacets extended).
  IEEE rounding is `strconv.ParseFloat`/`FormatFloat` at bitSize 32/64
  (floatingPointRound-conformant); overflow‚Üí¬±INF and underflow‚Üísigned-0 are
  VALID, not rejections.
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî the datatypes lane selector still claims only the lexical/
  facet cohorts it has cases for; widening it to route float/double through
  strict is #57's job (arbiter to confirm via GOXSD_RATCHET=1).
- Verdicts: Arbiter round 1 REJECT ‚Äî one blocking [T8] doc-drift finding:
  `builtin/strict/doc.go`'s `# Current coverage` paragraph and its
  whiteSpace-stage example still described float/double as future-milestone
  work, contradicting the already-updated `New` godoc and the dispatch switch
  (`go doc ./builtin/strict` rendered the stale "unimplemented" claim first).
  Everything else verified spec-exact for the record: the Incomparable/bounds
  fix, Eq-vs-Identical independence, special-literal grammar (`+NaN`/`-NaN`
  rejected), overflow/underflow-as-valid, the capability surface, and no new
  exported identifiers (`go doc ./builtin/strict` byte-identical to main).
  Mason repair round (commit fa2077e, doc.go only, +12/-11) reconciled both
  doc sections (float/double dropped from future work; float/double added to
  the whiteSpace=collapse example). Arbiter round 2 ACCEPT, no findings ‚Äî full
  gate green (build/test/vet/golangci-lint 0 issues, conformance), and
  `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` produced no expectation-file changes (per-lane movement
  unchanged). The datatypes lane doesn't yet route float/double (#57's job),
  so this cohort is proven via `value/backendtest.Run(strict.New())` and by
  `builtin.Seed`'s `MissingPrimitivesError` set shrinking by exactly `float` +
  `double` ‚Äî not by conformance cases. Commits: 1d465da (implementation) +
  fa2077e (doc repair).
- Surprises: the load-bearing branch was already present in the facet pipeline
  from #45 but had never fired ‚Äî `boundFacet.CheckValue`'s `value.Incomparable`
  arm would have panicked, since the totally-ordered decimal cohort never
  produces an Incomparable result. float/double is the first primitive with a
  genuine partial order, so this issue is where that latent panic converts to a
  real bounds-exclusion outcome.
- Friction: the round-1 REJECT was pure doc drift ‚Äî the implementation commit's
  own log/PR text claimed "doc.go coverage updated" while doc.go's
  `# Current coverage` section was in fact left stale, costing one repair round.
- Next: #57 (datatypes lane widening) can now route/decide float/double
  instances through strict. No other follow-ups identified at landing.

## 2026-07-13 ‚Äî #81 ‚Äî datatypes lane widened to the integer-family cohort

- Shipped: the datatypes conformance lane now claims the MS Facets instance
  cases for xs:integer and its twelve narrowings (int/long/short/byte,
  unsignedInt/Long/Short/Byte, nonNegativeInteger/nonPositiveInteger/
  positiveInteger/negativeInteger). Test-only change in conformance/datatypes.go:
  the `facetsCase` regex gains a shared `facetsBaseTypes` alternation, the
  execFacetsCase cohort guard becomes `strictGoverns` (walks the base chain so a
  derived builtin whose nearest mapped ancestor is xs:decimal is accepted), and
  the synthesized leaf's {primitive type definition} now resolves via
  `primitiveOfType` to the true primitive (xs:decimal) instead of the immediate
  builtin base. No library code, no new value type, no new Mapping entry, no new
  exported symbol ‚Äî the warden's binding conditions.
- Confirmation, not new machinery: the generated builtin table already carries
  each type's fixed fractionDigits=0, fixed pattern=[\-+]?[0-9]+ and per-type
  min/maxInclusive bounds, and the generic strict facet pipeline
  (ValidateLexical ‚Üí governingMapping walks int‚Üílong‚Üíinteger‚Üídecimal) validates
  them end-to-end unchanged. Verified with throwaway DIAG tests before wiring:
  all 310 claimed cases pass, and the polarities land on the right rule IDs ‚Äî
  "5.0"/"1e2" ‚Üí cvc-pattern-valid (NOT cvc-fractionDigits-valid), out-of-range
  (int 2147483648, byte 128/-129, unsignedLong max+1/-1, positiveInteger 0,
  negativeInteger 0) ‚Üí cvc-max/minInclusive-valid; "+007", "-0" accepted.
- Spec: ¬ß2.2.1 Identity note; ¬ß3.4.13‚Äì¬ß3.4.25 (integer family = decimal
  restrictions); cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4; cvc-max/minInclusive-valid
  ¬ß4.3.7.3/¬ß4.3.10.3; st-restrict-facets ¬ß3.16.6.4 (widest-space governing
  mapping). Oracle GROUNDING + warden pre-flight posted on #81.

  untouched (per the #80 convention the same cases stay recorded there as stub
  fails). The odd multi-element case Facets/int/test111092.xml stays an honest
  instance-lane gap (does not fit the single-<foo> shape).
- Tests: no new unit tests ‚Äî the widening is exercised by the 310 conformance
  cases themselves (the DIAG probes that proved the rule IDs were throwaway,
  deleted before handoff per WORKFLOW).
- Surprises: none ‚Äî the warden's "already wired" hypothesis held exactly; the
  only real change was the cohort guard, which previously asked strict to map
  the base DIRECTLY (false for a derived builtin) instead of walking to its
  governing ancestor.
- Friction: none.

## 2026-07-13 ‚Äî issue #87 ‚Äî hoisted the backend-generic facet pipeline into value

- Shipped: moved the whole backend-generic facet pipeline out of builtin/strict
  into the shared value package. New value/facets.go (ValidateLexical, compile,
  governingMapping, declaringMapping, the pattern/enum/bound/digits/length
  checkers) and value/whitespace.go (whiteSpace enum, normalizeWhiteSpace/
  replaceSpace/collapseSpace, and a NEW effectiveWhiteSpace). builtin/strict's
  facets.go and whitespace.go deleted; strict now only supplies the per-type
  mappings the pipeline drives. value gains two leaf imports (regex, xsderr) ‚Äî
  no cycle (both are leaves w.r.t. value/xsd/builtin).
- The blocker was strict's whiteSpaceOfType ‚Üí primitiveOf ‚Üí whiteSpaceOf, which
  read builtin.Types (builtin imports value ‚Üí cycle). Replaced with
  effectiveWhiteSpace(st): it scans st.EffectiveFacets() for FacetWhiteSpace and
  maps the {value} string to the mode enum, panicking on absence (the atomic
  cohort's existing documented precondition). This is a CORRECTNESS UPGRADE, not
  just cycle-avoidance: reading the resolved whiteSpace off EffectiveFacets
  honors a legal derived whiteSpace override under the ordinary same-kind replace
  overlay (¬ß3.16.6.4), which the old builtin.Types-only primitive lookup could
  not; oracle confirmed behaviorally identical for the fixed decimal/boolean/
  string cohort (¬ß4.3.6.1 f-w-fixed) on #87.
- Deleted (not moved) normalizeForParse/whiteSpaceOf/parseWhiteSpace/primitiveOf
  ‚Äî no production consumer (warden pre-flight #1/#3). Test re-homing: the
  surviving whitespace transform + zero-mode-panic tests became white-box tests
  in package value (value/whitespace_test.go) alongside a new effectiveWhiteSpace
  test (inherit + legal override + no-facet panic); the deleted-function tests
  (TestWhiteSpaceOf, TestNormalizeForParseThenParse) were dropped. facets_test.go
  stayed in package strict, repointed to value.ValidateLexical; its newPrim now
  carries the primitive's own whiteSpace facet (as builtin.Seed does) and derive
  walks Base()/IsPrimitive inline (primitiveOf is gone).
- Repointed conformance/datatypes.go's ValidateLexical call and prose to value.*
  (strict import retained for strict.New()); updated builtin/strict/doc.go's
  whiteSpace-stage prose and docs/ARCHITECTURE.md's value import line (+regex).
- Spec: ¬ß4.3.6 rf-whiteSpace/dt-whiteSpace, ¬ß4.3.6.1 f-w-fixed, ¬ß3.16.6.4
  key-facets-overlay, ¬ß3.16.7.4 (built-in primitive {facets}), ¬ß4.1.5
  cos-applicable-facets; pipeline rule IDs unchanged (cvc-pattern-valid,
  cvc-enumeration-valid, cvc-*Inclusive/Exclusive-valid, cvc-totalDigits/
  fractionDigits-valid, cvc-length/minLength/maxLength-valid).
- Verdicts: Warden pre-flight APPROVE WITH CHANGES (delete-not-move the dead
  helpers, an explicit test re-homing plan, the docs/ARCHITECTURE.md update) ‚Äî
  all three discharged above. Arbiter ACCEPT, no findings: full gate green and
  the GOXSD_RATCHET=1 run confirmed the ratchet UNCHANGED in every lane
  (datatypes 506/511 pass both before and after), zero expectations-file

  flagged a phantom expectations change (false alarm), then re-diffed against

- Ratchet: unchanged. Full gate green (build/test/vet/lint); conformance PASS,
  datatypes 506/511 identical before and after; expectations untouched.

## 2026-07-13 ‚Äî issue #83 ‚Äî xs:hexBinary and xs:base64Binary primitives mapped

- Shipped (mason 7a79e94 + ratchet 5c228a2): strict backend now maps the two
  binary primitives (new builtin/strict/binary.go). Both value types are
  []byte-backed and unexported, satisfying value.Lengthed (OCTET count per
  cvc-length-valid ¬ß4.3.1.3 ‚Äî not character count), value.Eq (byte-wise), and
  value.Canonical, but deliberately NOT value.Ordered (both fundamentally
  unordered per ¬ß3.3.15.3 / ¬ß3.3.16.3). parseHexBinary rejects odd-length and
  non-hex lexicals against `^([0-9a-fA-F]{2})*$` and canonicalizes to uppercase
  (f-hexBinaryCanonical); parseBase64Binary validates the full spec grammar
  including the restricted final-quantum character subset (B16char / B04char)
  that a naive StdEncoding decode would wave through, canonicalizing via
  StdEncoding. Rejections are tagged cvc-datatype-valid via xsderr.
  tools/backendtestgen extended and value/backendtest/gen_vectors.go regenerated
  with spec-derived vectors (not hand-typed). conformance/datatypes.go's lexical
  selector now admits the hexBinary/base64Binary cases and the fallbackPrimitives
  doc comment was corrected to 8 mapped / 12 fallback = 20 total.
- Spec: xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß3.3.15 (hexBinary) / ¬ß3.3.16 (base64Binary) ‚Äî value
  space is finite-length octet sequences, lexical spaces are the hex and base64
  grammars respectively; length is measured in octets (cvc-length-valid ¬ß4.3.1.3);
  both fundamental facets ordered=false (¬ß3.3.15.3 / ¬ß3.3.16.3). cvc-datatype-valid
  ¬ß4.1.4 for lexical rejection. Same precedent as #82's anyURI011 for the
  list-variety honest-fail gaps.
- Ratchet: datatypes lane 516/522 ‚Üí 520/528 pass (+6 cases: +4 pass, +2
  honest-fail), recorded by the arbiter via GOXSD_RATCHET=1 in commit 5c228a2.
  Pass: hexBinary001, hexBinary003, hexBinary004, base64Binary001. Honest fail:
  hexBinary002 and base64Binary002 are list-of-binary variety cases that resolve
  to a non-seeded list type strict does not govern ‚Äî the same class of gap as
  anyURI011 (#82) and boolean018, not regressions or bugs. No other lane changed.
- Gate: build/test/vet/lint all green; conformance PASS. Arbiter independently
  re-verified the hex/base64 grammar handling against the spec (the base64 final-
  quantum restriction in particular) before accepting.
- Surprises: none ‚Äî the base64 final-character subset validation was the one
  substantive subtlety (a plain decoder accepts trailing bits the spec forbids),
  handled explicitly in parseBase64Binary.
- Friction: none.
- Next: none ‚Äî self-contained. The remaining unmapped primitives (dates/times,
  QName/NOTATION, list varieties) stay deferred to their own backends.

## 2026-07-14 ‚Äî issue #103 ‚Äî xs:dateTime anchors the date/time family (also closes #89)

- Shipped (commit 5436a57): builtin/strict/datetime.go ‚Äî the seven-property
  temporal value model (¬ß3.3.7.1: year/month/day/hour/minute/second/
  timezoneOffset) as `dateTimeVal{year *big.Int, month, day, hour, minute int,
  second *big.Rat, tzOffset *int}`. Calendar math reuses duration.go's
  `daysFromCivil` (Hinnant days_from_civil) rather than duplicating it
  (PRINCIPLES 4). `tzOffset == nil` is the SOLE encoding of timezone-absence ‚Äî
  no redundant `hasTimezone` bool (D3). Wired xs:dateTime into strict.go's
  Mapping. This also resolves #89: `value.TimezoneAware`, previously an exported
  interface with zero implementers, now has a real implementer (dateTimeVal) and
  consumer (the `capTimezoneAware` backendtest capability). dateTime is the
  anchor of the family; time/date/gYearMonth/gYear/gMonthDay/gDay/gMonth and
  dateTimeStamp are explicit future siblings, not implemented here.
- Spec: xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß3.3.7.1 (seven-property value space), ¬ß3.3.7.2
  (nt-dateTimeRep lexical space; endOfDayFrag "24:00:00"), ¬ßD.2.1 (the ¬±840-min
  / ¬±14h dual-imputation partial order over timezone-absent vs -aware operands),
  con-dateTime-dayValue (leap-year / day-of-month validity), cvc-datatype-valid
  ¬ß4.1.4 for lexical + semantic rejection. explicitTimezone ¬ß4.3.14 grounded as
  out of scope for this issue. Applicable facets leave dateTime as
  Ordered/Eq/Identical/Canonical + TimezoneAware, deliberately not Lengthed/
  DigitCounted/Scaled.
- Ratchet: datatypes lane 576 ‚Üí 586 pass (588 ‚Üí 599 cases); +10 dateTime
  instance cases now pass (dateTime001/002/003/004/005/006/007/008/010/011).
  dateTime013 recorded as an honest structural gap ‚Äî a multi-attribute document
  shape the lane's single-primitive-element executor doesn't decide, not a
  dateTime-mapping bug. 0 regressions, 0 vanished. Arbiter ran GOXSD_RATCHET=1.
- Gate: build/test/vet/lint all green; `go generate ./...` drift-free.
- Decisions: (1) con-dateTime-dayValue leap-year/day-of-month validation is
  folded into cvc-datatype-valid rejection, not a separate facet check, so
  regex-passing-but-semantically-invalid lexicals like `2023-02-30` are rejected
  at parse. (2) endOfDayFrag ("24:00:00") is normalized at parse ‚Äî hour-24 is
  carried into the next calendar day, so hour is never stored as 24. (3) `Cmp`
  implements the ¬ßD.2.1 dual-imputation partial order, correctly BYPASSING
  imputation when both operands agree on timezone-presence. (4) `Eq` is derived
  from `Cmp==Equal` while `Identical` is a separate structural comparison ‚Äî they
  genuinely diverge (e.g. `2002-10-10T12:00:00-05:00` and `...T17:00:00Z` are Eq
  but not Identical, since Identical also compares the stored timezoneOffset).
  (5) Field shape was mandated by a warden pre-flight BEFORE code: the initial
  sketch's `tzOffsetMinutes int` + `hasTimezone bool` and plain `year int` were
  both revised (to `*int` and `*big.Int`) ‚Äî illegal states made unrepresentable.
  (6) Shared test infra: `capTimezoneAware` added to value/backendtest/kit.go is
  facet-driven (keys off vectors listing `explicitTimezone`), so it generalizes
  automatically to future date/time-family siblings ‚Äî warden approved this as
  the correct layer.
- Generator: tools/backendtestgen/parse.go gained an independent `parseDateTime`
  oracle (extracts the spec's own equivalent-regex fenced block plus a full
  day-of-month validity oracle, so generated invalid vectors include the
  regex-passing-but-semantically-invalid cases); value/backendtest/gen_vectors.go
  regenerated via `go generate`, drift-free. conformance/datatypes.go's lexical
  cohort regex extended to claim dateTimeNNN.xml; fallbackPrimitives comment
  updated (9‚Üí10 primitives now strict-mapped).
- Verdicts: oracle grounding (GROUNDING: comment on #103 ‚Äî seven-property model,
  nt-dateTimeRep, explicitTimezone out-of-scope, timeOnTimeline order); warden
  pre-flight (mandated the two field-shape revisions above); mason (one commit,
  5436a57); warden diff review APPROVE, one non-blocking cosmetic doc-comment nit
  at datetime.go:184/205 (stale copy-pasted identifier in a comment, unexported
  so not lint-flagged); arbiter ACCEPT, full gate green, ratchet run.
- Next / deferred (for /backlog or the post-land pass): the remaining
  seven-property siblings (time, date, gYearMonth, gYear, gMonthDay, gDay,
  gMonth) and dateTimeStamp are explicit fast-follow candidates per #103's own
  text ("carve them as fast siblings once this anchor lands"); the cosmetic
  doc-comment nit at datetime.go ("secondCanonicalFragment" vs the actual
  "dateTimeSecondFragment") is a trivial fix-on-next-touch, not its own issue;
  `explicitTimezone` facet checking (cvc-explicitTimezone-valid) remains out of
  scope ‚Äî value/facets.go still marks it "out of this runner's scope" ‚Äî a future
  issue is needed to wire the generic facet pipeline to check it against
  TimezoneAware-implementing values.

  branches that compose real work but aren't `wip/issue-<N>`-named, so never
  get PR'd and are invisible to the `develop` skill's WIP survey (the exact
  failure that stranded T6 on `meta/retro-2026-07-12`). This landing recovers
  the one stranded branch; #112 owns the systemic fix.

## 2026-07-14 ‚Äî issue #104 ‚Äî wrong-path write investigation: not a harness bug

- Investigated the #84 corruption (root `README.md` clobbered with the
  expectations-README text; six stray root `ber/datatypes/instance/json/
  schema/xpath.txt`). Traced every write in `conformance/`: the ratchet's
  only writer is `WriteExpectations` (expectations.go), called by
  `runConformanceLane` with `laneFile(name)` ‚Üí `filepath.Join(expectationsDir,
  name+".txt")`, `expectationsDir = "testdata/expectations"`. No code anywhere
  in the harness (or under `tools/`, or any shell script ‚Äî there are none)
  writes `README.md` or copies lane files to cwd.
- The path is package-dir-relative (like `suiteRoot`), which is safe under
  `go test`: Go always runs a package's tests with its source dir as cwd, so
  the join resolves to `conformance/testdata/expectations/` regardless of
  where `go test ./conformance` is invoked from. Not a cwd bug; not fixed
  (STYLE: don't invent a fix for a non-bug, don't add a new path-anchoring
  convention where the existing relative-constant one is correct).
- Guard verified: `git status` clean before and after
  `GOXSD_RATCHET=1 go test ./conformance -run TestConformance -count=1` from
  the repo root ‚Äî scores unmoved, no root `*.txt`, `README.md` untouched.
- Conclusion: the corruption fingerprint (README overwritten with the
  expectations README *and* all six lane files present at root) matches a
  manual `cp conformance/testdata/expectations/* .` run from the repo root
  during the #84 review session ‚Äî an external agent shell action, not the Go
  harness. Documented on #104; no code change.
- Ratchet: unchanged. Next: close #104 with this evidence.

## 2026-07-15 ‚Äî issue #108 ‚Äî wire the explicitTimezone facet into the value-facet pipeline

- Shipped (commit 58dd171): value/facets.go now checks the explicitTimezone
  facet against TimezoneAware values. `xsd.FacetExplicitTimezone` was split
  out of `compile()`'s skip-case (it had been grouped with `FacetAssertions`
  and silently skipped) into a real unexported `explicitTimezoneFacet`
  `ValueFacet` checker, with a `tzRequirement` enum and a
  `newExplicitTimezoneFacet` constructor. The checker enforces the three-way
  branch (required ‚áí non-absent ¬∑timezoneOffset¬∑, prohibited ‚áí absent,
  optional ‚áí always valid) against `value.TimezoneAware` values. Malformed
  {value} tokens are rejected at construction; a candidate lacking
  `TimezoneAware` panics (schema-construction-error convention, matching
  `boundFacet`/`digitsFacet`/`lengthFacet`). `FacetAssertions` keeps its own
  skip-case (a separate later stage, unrelated).
- Also fixed 5 stale "¬ß4.3.15" ‚Üí "¬ß4.3.14" citations on the
  `value.TimezoneAware` capability found along the way: value/value.go,
  builtin/strict/datetime.go, builtin/strict/strict.go,
  builtin/strict/datetime_test.go, value/backendtest/kit.go.
- Tests: builtin/strict/facets_test.go ‚Äî TestExplicitTimezoneFacet
  (required/prohibited/optional √ó tz/no-tz, dateTime backend) and
  TestExplicitTimezoneFacetMalformed.
- Spec: cvc-explicitTimezone-valid (xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß4.3.14.3, the three-way
  branch); {value} domain {required,prohibited,optional} (¬ß4.3.14.1);
  applicability is the date/time family only per ¬ß4.1.5 cos-applicable-facets
  (explicitly NOT duration). Oracle grounding posted verbatim on #108.
- No new exported identifiers (STYLE T5/T8 clean ‚Äî arbiter confirmed
  independently against the exported-surface diff).
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî this facet exercises no currently-tracked conformance
  lane, so `conformance/testdata/expectations/` is untouched (empty diff).
  Arbiter ran GOXSD_RATCHET=1 and the outcome was UNCHANGED.
- Verdicts: arbiter ACCEPT, first round, no repair needed; full gate green
  (build/test/vet/lint/conformance).
- Note: mason had bundled a premature LOG entry into its own commit; the
  orchestrator stripped it (ab3d5ba) per WORKFLOW.md role separation ‚Äî LOG
  entries are the chronicler's job at the land step, written after the verdict
