## 2026-07-15 ‚Äî issue #106 ‚Äî wider string-family Facets cohort (language/Name/NCName/NMTOKEN)

- Widened the `conformance` datatypes lane's `facetsBaseTypes` alternation to
  include `language|Name|NCName|NMTOKEN` (60 MS Facets instance cases, 15 each).
  All four derive from `token` (NCName via `Name`) and resolve to the xs:string
  primitive via the existing `strictGoverns`/`primitiveOfType` chain (#81) ‚Äî zero
  new resolution logic. Datatypes lane claimed cases 599 ‚Üí 659.
- The issue's Notes assumed the seeding+plumbing already worked; it did NOT for
  three of the four types (verified, not assumed). Three defects were uncovered
  and fixed as the minimal correct thing to meet the acceptance criteria:
  1. **regex `\i`/`\c`/`\I`/`\C` were unsupported** (rejected as "XML NameChar
     class not supported"). These MultiCharEsc (Datatypes ¬ßG.4.2.5) are required
     by Name (`\i\c*`), NMTOKEN (`\c+`), NCName (`[\i-[:]][\c-[:]]*`). Added
     `nameStartSet`/`nameCharSet` (XML 1.0 5th-ed NameStartChar/NameChar
     productions [4]/[4a], transcribed from docs/specs/md/xml.md) to
     regex/class.go and wired both the atom (regex.go) and character-class
     (classparse.go) parse sites, including class-subtraction bases `[\i-[:]]`.
     Oracle-grounded (posted on #106); no exported surface change.
  2. **NCName's generated pattern was the prose intersection**
     `\i\c* ‚à© [\i-[:]][\c-[:]]*` (¬ß3.4.7.1 effective value-space notation), not a
     compilable regex. Added a post-processing pass in
     tools/hfnextract/builtins that reduces a ‚à©-intersection pattern to the
     type's OWN step operands (subtracting the base type's operands): NCName ‚Üí
     `[\i-[:]][\c-[:]]*`; ID/IDREF/ENTITY (derived from NCName, no new pattern) ‚Üí
     no own pattern (inherit via chain). EffectiveFacets re-ANDs the inherited
     Name pattern across the step (¬ß4.3.4.2 xr-pattern, the cross-step AND #94
     built). Guarded to only the ‚à© cases, so the integer family's own patterns
     are untouched. Regenerated builtin/gen_typespec.go (4-row diff).
  3. **NMTOKEN cases carry the tested value in an attribute** (`attrTest`), not
     `<foo>` element content, so the reader validated the wrong value.
     `readFacetsCase`/`decodeRestriction` now capture the enclosing
     `xsd:attribute` name and read the matching instance attribute.
- Spec: cvc-pattern-valid (¬ß4.3.4.4), cvc-datatype-valid (¬ß4.1.4), xr-pattern
  (¬ß4.3.4.2), MultiCharEsc `\i`/`\c` (¬ßG.4.2.5).
- Tests: conformance TestDatatypesFacetsWideStringFamily (both polarities across
  all four cohorts, attribute-carried NMTOKEN values, and a direct NCName
  colon-rejection via the value pipeline asserting cvc-pattern-valid ‚Äî the corpus
  has no colon case); regex TestNameCharEscapes (\i/\c/\I/\C standalone + NCName
  class subtraction). Removed the now-stale regex "unsupported-name-escape" case.
- No new exported identifiers. Full gate green (build/test/vet/lint/conformance).
- Verdicts: arbiter ACCEPT (mason's implementation at ff2e8da). The arbiter
  endorsed the broader-than-scoped change: the issue framed this as "test-only
  cohort widening in package conformance" (Surface: none expected), but three
  cross-package fixes ‚Äî regex engine `\i\c\I\C` (MultiCharEsc) support, builtin
  generator pattern-intersection resolution, and conformance NMTOKEN
  attribute-value reading ‚Äî proved necessary to decide 3 of the 4 cohorts for
  the right reason, all justified as tightly-coupled prerequisites. Fix #2 also
  corrects ID/IDREF/ENTITY's (previously broken, redundant) own pattern ‚Äî
  collateral but strictly more correct; no conformance lane decides those types.
- Ratchet: datatypes lane 599 ‚Üí 659 (+60), Facets/{language,Name,NCName,NMTOKEN}
  cohort, 15 cases each; nothing regressed. Ratcheted by the arbiter and
  committed separately as d5a4b71 (expectations are arbiter-only).

## 2026-07-15 ‚Äî issue #109 ‚Äî map the seven-property date/time siblings (time/date/gYearMonth/gYear/gMonthDay/gDay/gMonth)

- Mapped the seven remaining seven-property temporal primitives in
  `builtin/strict` as thin lexical projections over the shared value model, order
  and timezone machinery `datetime.go` established for xs:dateTime (#103).
  `xs:dateTimeStamp` was explicitly OUT OF SCOPE this session (sequenced later).
- Warden pre-flight ("revise") drove two load-bearing design choices, both
  followed: (1) the shared `¬∑timeOnTimeline¬∑` filler is `sevenProp`, an
  unexported struct with **nil-as-absence pointer** fields + an `instant()`
  method ‚Äî no bool presence flags (illegal states unrepresentable, STYLE D6/T7);
  (2) `dateTimeVal.instant()` was refactored to build an all-present `sevenProp`
  whose fillers are no-ops, so its instant stays **bit-identical** to the
  pre-refactor `daysFromCivil` computation (the dateTime ratchet-safety point).
  The filler resolves absent props to the spec's 1972-12-31T00:00:00 civil date
  (year‚Üí1972, month‚Üí12, day‚Üí`daysInMonth` of the filler month, h/m/s‚Üí0, verified
  against ¬ßE.3.4 line 6060) then feeds the completed civil tuple into the EXISTING
  `daysFromCivil` core ‚Äî NOT ¬ßE.3.4's alternate ordinal arithmetic.
- Per-type value structs (`timeVal`/`dateVal`/`gYearMonthVal`/`gYearVal`/
  `gMonthDayVal`/`gDayVal`/`gMonthVal`) carry only always-present properties as
  plain scalars plus `tzOffset *int` (nil==absent), the dateTimeVal precedent.
  Each has its own anchored lexical regex (transcribed from ¬ß3.3.8‚Äì¬ß3.3.14's
  "equivalent regular expression" spans), `parseX`/`canonicalX`/`Canonical`/
  `Eq`/`Identical`/`Cmp`/`HasTimezone`. `Cmp` reuses a new shared `cmpInstants`
  (the ¬±840-min dual-imputation partial order, factored out of dateTimeVal.Cmp).
  Day-of-month checks: `date` year-dependent (con-date-dayValue ¬ß3.3.9.1),
  `gMonthDay` year-FREE (con-gMonthDay-dayValue ¬ß3.3.12.1 ‚Äî `--02-29` always
  valid); `gDay`/`gYear`/`gYearMonth`/`gMonth` carry no day-value rule. Fixed
  `gMonth`'s canonical map to use `¬∑month¬∑` (spec's "gM's ¬∑day¬∑" is a
  transcription artifact ‚Äî PRINCIPLES 25). Swept the `secondCanonicalFragment`
  ‚Üí `dateTimeSecondFragment` doc-comment nit flagged on the #103 thread.
- Registered all seven in `strict.go`'s `Mapping` switch; updated `New()` doc
  and `doc.go` "Current coverage". strict now maps 17 of 20 primitives (was 10);
  `fallbackPrimitives` covers the remaining 3 (precisionDecimal, QName, NOTATION).
- Vectors are spec-derived, never hand-typed (PRINCIPLES 26/27): extended
  `tools/backendtestgen` with seven `parseX` extractors + independent canonical
  oracles (day-value violations decided via the full oracle, like dateTime), a
  shared `gregorianRegex` span-extractor, and pin tests. Regenerated
  `value/backendtest/gen_vectors.go` via `go generate` (TestCommittedUpToDate +
  TestDeterministic green). Applicable facets = the 9 dateTime facets (no length
  family), sourced from the shared builtin parser.
- Conformance: widened the datatypes lexical selector to claim
  `{time,date,gYearMonth,gYear,gMonthDay,gDay,gMonth}NNN.xml`; updated lane +
  fallback docs. Sanity run (mason, NOT the ratchet): datatypes lane 659 ‚Üí 716
  claimed cases, observed pass 646 ‚Üí 700 (+54), New=57, Regressed=0 ‚Äî arbiter to
  record via GOXSD_RATCHET=1.
- Spec: cvc-datatype-valid (¬ß4.1.4), con-date-dayValue (¬ß3.3.9.1),
  con-gMonthDay-dayValue (¬ß3.3.12.1), vp-timeOnTimeline (¬ßE.3.4), the seven
  vp-*LexRep/vp-*CanRep maps (¬ßE.3.5/¬ßE.3.6), cos-applicable-facets (¬ß4.1.5),
  ¬ßD.2.1 order.
- Zero new exported identifiers. Full gate green (build/test/vet/lint/conformance
  read-only). Tests: `builtin/strict/gregorian_test.go` (round-trips, rejects,
  the ¬ß3.3.13.1 gDay order anomalies + ¬ß3.3.12.1 gMonthDay tz anomaly verbatim,
  Eq/Identical divergence, cross-type Incomparable, HasTimezone, not-Lengthed,
  foreign-value guardrail); generator pin tests for all seven.

## 2026-07-15 ‚Äî issue #111 ‚Äî process: byte-identical is not an acceptance criterion for regeneration

- Shipped: one new bullet in the "GitHub conventions" list of docs/WORKFLOW.md,
  immediately after the issue-body-contents bullet. It tells issue authors that
  for an issue regenerating a spec-derived table (`xsderr/catalog.go`, the spec
  `.md` files, any generated Go table), "regenerated output is byte-identical to
  the committed file" must NOT be an acceptance criterion unless a spec grep
  first confirms the committed table already holds every member the widened
  generator will admit. Regeneration correctly ADDS previously-missed entries
  (often the point), so byte-identity is usually vacuous or self-contradictory;
  the right criterion is "the regenerated diff is additive-only and every added
  entry is a genuine spec member," verified by grep.
- Motivation: recurring pattern in the LOG ‚Äî landings routinely note "`go
  generate` twice byte-identical" as evidence, which is correct as an idempotency
  check but wrong if smuggled in as the acceptance criterion for a generator
  WIDENING (e.g. #3's rulecat prefix-family widen from 126‚Üí132, #12's F&O code
  harvest ‚Äî both ADDED entries a byte-identical criterion would have forbidden).
- Spec: n/a (process/docs only).
- Ratchet: unchanged (docs only; no Go code, no conformance lanes touched).
- Decisions: WORKFLOW.md (the normative issue-body doc) alone satisfies the
  acceptance criterion; the cartographer issue template (.claude/agents/
  cartographer.md) is deliberately left untouched ‚Äî one authoritative home, no
  duplicate prose to drift. Left the ratchet-integrity section and CLAUDE.md
  alone (those change only via a human-filed issue).
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint green (docs-only change, trivially).
- Next: land via PR squash-merge (`Closes #111`).

## 2026-07-15 ‚Äî issue #112 ‚Äî recovered 9 stranded log entries + PLAN.md status from 9 orphaned branches

- Shipped: swept every remote head against `origin/main`; found `meta/retro-2026-07-12`
  (3 commits) and 8 `claude/optimistic-bardeen-*` branches (one per daily `/backlog`
  run, 2026-07-08 through 2026-07-15), none merged into main. Cross-checked each
  touched file against current main: the STYLE.md T6 / mason.md T6 checklist /
  ARCHITECTURE.md pure-leaf wording from the retro branch were already recovered by
  other means (#88 and/or direct edits) ‚Äî only the LOG entries and a PLAN.md status
  paragraph were genuinely missing. Recovered all 9 missing LOG entries verbatim
  (chronological order) and the 2026-07-15 PLAN.md M1‚ÄìM4 status snapshot (adjusted:
  #111 already landed by the time of this recovery, doesn't change the M3 status
  text; issue references #114/#115/#116/#122/#123/#124/#125 all verified still open
  and accurate).
- Decisions: did NOT hand-merge the 7 earlier (now-superseded) daily PLAN.md
  snapshots from the other 7 orphaned branches ‚Äî each is a point-in-time ready-queue
  narrative superseded same-day or next-day by the following `/backlog` run; only
  the LOG entries (irreplaceable dated audit trail) and the single latest PLAN.md
  snapshot were worth recovering by hand. The 9 source branches are left in place,
  unmerged and un-deleted (no session force-deletes a remote ref); their content is
  now on `main` via this issue's PR, so a future `/backlog` branch-namespace sweep
  can retire them as superseded.
- Root cause (Part b): `docs/WORKFLOW.md` described `/backlog`/`/retro`/`/ratchet`
  as committing straight to `main`, and the three command files just said "commit,
  push" ‚Äî neither said what to do when a direct push to `main` isn't possible or
  isn't taken, so every one of these sessions landed on an ad-hoc branch nothing
  ever merged. Fixed by requiring the same PR + squash-merge landing wip/issue- work
  already uses (docs/WORKFLOW.md + backlog.md/retro.md/ratchet.md).
- Ratchet: unchanged (docs/log only; no Go code, no conformance files touched).
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint all green; conformance green; no code changed.
- Verdicts: Arbiter ACCEPT (verdict at
  https://github.com/kud360/goxsd8/issues/112#issuecomment-4980918573) ‚Äî full
  gate green, no repair round needed.
- Next: a future `/backlog` branch-namespace sweep can note the 9 source branches
  as superseded-by-#112 for human/agent triage; none are deleted by this session.

## 2026-07-15 ‚Äî issue #114 ‚Äî QName/NOTATION strict mappings shipped

- Shipped (commit 332121b): builtin/strict/qname.go ‚Äî real value.Mappings for xs:QName (¬ß3.3.18)
  and xs:NOTATION (¬ß3.3.19), joining the dispatch switch in strict.go. Distinct
  unexported value types qnameVal/notationVal ({space, local} tuple), each
  value.Eq (tuple equality, never cross-matching the sibling type ‚Äî mirrors
  hexBinaryVal/base64BinaryVal) and value.Lengthed. Context-dependent Parse
  resolves the prefix (empty prefix = default namespace) via value.Context;
  malformed grammar or an unresolvable prefix ‚Üí cvc-datatype-valid (¬ß4.1.4).
  NCName grammar reused via regex.Translate(`[\i-[:]][\c-[:]]*`, FlavorXSD) so
  the NameStartChar/NameChar sets stay generated, not hand-typed (PRINCIPLES
  26/27). Mapping.Canonical is nil for both (spec defines no canonical form).
  Tests: builtin/strict/qname_test.go (fake map-backed Context; prefix
  resolution, unbound-prefix + nil-ctx rejection, default-namespace, malformed
  grammar, no-Canonical, not-Ordered, Len, QName‚âÝNOTATION cross-Eq).
- Spec: cvc-datatype-valid (¬ß4.1.4); ¬ß3.3.18/¬ß3.3.19 value/lexical spaces and
  context-dependent mapping; ¬ß4.3.1.3 clause 1.3 (length no-op for QName/
  NOTATION); cos-applicable-facets ¬ß4.1.5. NOTATION's "declared in current
  schema"/enumeration-required constraint deliberately NOT enforced in the leaf
  Parse (facet/Structures concern).
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî the conformance datatypes selector is NOT widened to

## 2026-07-16 ‚Äî #115 precisionDecimal strict mapping ‚Äî shipped

- Shipped: builtin/strict/precisiondecimal.go ‚Äî xs:precisionDecimal mapped to a
  real value.Mapping. Unexported precisionDecimalVal as a discriminated union
  (pdKind: numeric | posInf | negInf | nan); the (coefficient, scale, sign)
  triple lives only in the numeric arm so "NaN with a scale"/"INF with a sign"
  are unrepresentable (warden guardrail). Implements value.Ordered (partial:
  -INF < numeric < +INF, NaN incomparable incl. itself), value.Eq (scale-blind
  via reduced big.Rat numericalValue), value.Identical (scale+sign-SENSITIVE;
  NaN‚â°NaN), value.Scaled (scale absent for specials), value.DigitCounted
  (totalDigits = coefficient digit count incl. trailing zeros, ¬ß4.1 formula
  collapses to D; fractionDigits inert), value.Canonical (¬ß6 5-step: specials,
  bare numeral, decimal-point trailing-zero pad, scientific for negative scale /
  out-of-range). Spec: ¬ß3.1/¬ß3.2/¬ß3.3/¬ß4.1/¬ß6, PRINCIPLES 18.
- strict.New() Mapping now registers precisionDecimal ‚Üí strict covers ALL 20
  builtin primitives. Consequence: builtin.Seed(strict.New()) no longer returns
  a MissingPrimitivesError. Retargeted strict_test.go: TestBackendUnmapped drops
  precisionDecimal, TestBackendCoverage adds it,
  TestSeedMissingShrinksByFloatDouble ‚Üí TestSeedCoversAllPrimitives (asserts Seed
  now succeeds with len(Types)+1 components). New precisiondecimal_test.go (9
  tests): lexical accept/reject (rejects INFINITY/inf/NAN/+NaN), canonical
  trailing-zero preservation (spec example table), Eq/Cmp quantum-blindness vs
  Identical scale-sensitivity, NaN incomparable-but-identical, totalDigits
  zero/special casing, Scale() absence for specials.
- Docs: builtin/strict/strict.go New() godoc + builtin/strict/doc.go "Current
  coverage" now list precisionDecimal and note the maxScale/minScale gap;
  conformance/datatypes.go fallbackPrimitives comments updated (strict now maps
  20/20, fallback fully redundant, retained as defensive floor). GAP(facet)
  marker for maxScale/minScale non-enforcement placed on precisionDecimalVal's
  doc in precisiondecimal.go.
- Scope held per warden pre-flight: did NOT touch xsd/simpletype.go FacetKind or
  value/facets.go ‚Äî maxScale/minScale enforcement is out of scope (cross-cutting
  enum extension), left as a documented GAP for a follow-up issue.
- Ratchet: unchanged. Guardrail-6 investigation: initialized testdata/xsdtests
  and confirmed the W3C suite DOES contain precisionDecimal Facets cases using
  maxScale/minScale (saxonData/PDecimal/*, ibmData/*/D3_3_4/*,
  saxonMeta/PDecimal.testSet, ibmMeta/precisionDecimal.testSet). BUT the
  conformance datatypes selector claims NO precisionDecimal case at all (grep of

  boolean/decimal/string/float/double/... and the integer/derived-string

  claims zero new cases and cannot make a maxScale/minScale case pass for the
  wrong reason. No expectations touched; non-ratchet TestConformance still green.

  maxScale/minScale enforcement follow-up issue referenced by the GAP marker.

  xs:string primitive, so strict's string mapping governs them with zero new

  playbook (for agents)" section of docs/WORKFLOW.md ‚Äî never snapshot or
  copy the working tree with ad-hoc `cp`/backup commands into or beside the
  repo root during conformance review, since a stray
  `cp conformance/testdata/expectations/* .` once clobbered the tracked root
  `README.md` and littered lane `*.txt` files at repo root (#104); if a
  working copy is genuinely needed, put it well outside the repo (the
  scratchpad dir) or use `git worktree`. Docs-only diff, +6 lines to
  docs/WORKFLOW.md, nothing else touched.
- Motivation: harvested from the #104 landing (2026-07-14). #104 root-caused
  the transient repo-root corruption during #84's conformance review as an
  external one-off manual `cp` from repo root ‚Äî NOT a Go harness bug ‚Äî and
  recommended a caution in agent-facing guidance rather than a harness change.
  This issue is that caution.
- Spec: n/a (process/docs only).
- Ratchet: unchanged (docs-only diff; nothing in conformance/testdata/
  expectations/ touched).

## 2026-07-16 ‚Äî issue #122 ‚Äî map xs:dateTimeStamp by aliasing dateTime's value model

- Shipped: `backend.Mapping` gains a `dateTimeStamp` case returning dateTime's
  mapping VERBATIM (`Parse: parseDateTime, Canonical: canonicalDateTime`).
  dateTimeStamp (¬ß3.4.28) is a restriction of dateTime whose lexical/canonical
  mapping IS dateTime's, restricted to the tz-present value subset (¬ß3.4.28.1) ‚Äî
  no independent representation exists. The tz-required constraint is enforced
  generically by the explicitTimezone facet pipeline (#108,
  cvc-explicitTimezone-valid ¬ß4.3.14), reading dateTimeVal's value.TimezoneAware;
  it is NOT re-checked in Parse (would double-encode, PRINCIPLES 4). The fixed
  facet defaults (whiteSpace=collapse, explicitTimezone=required) already lived
  in the generated typespec (builtin/gen_typespec.go:760), so no generator work.
- Tests (builtin/strict/datetimestamp_test.go): Mapping(dateTimeStamp) ok with
  non-nil Parse/Canonical and a tz-bearing round-trip; and the REAL seeded
  builtin dateTimeStamp type through value.ValidateLexical ‚Äî tz-bearing accepted,
  tz-absent rejected as cvc-explicitTimezone-valid (proves the generated fixed
  facet reaches enforcement for the actual seeded type, not just derive()-built).
- Conformance: widened the lexical-cohort regex (conformance/datatypes.go) to
  list dateTimeStamp for forward parity. FINDING: the checkout has ZERO
  msData/datatypes/dateTimeStampNNN.xml cases (only ibmMeta/dateTimeStamp.testSet
  metadata), so the alternative is inert today ‚Äî no lane movement. Documented a
  fail-open GAP at the regex + package doc: unlike every other cohort member,
  dateTimeStamp's Parse-only path (execLexicalCase ‚Üí parseDateTime) does NOT
  enforce the required timezone (that lives only in the facet cohort's
  value.ValidateLexical), so a future tz-absent dateTimeStamp case would be
  false-ACCEPTED and must instead move to the facet cohort. Flagged for arbiter.
- Spec: ¬ß3.4.28, ¬ß3.4.28.1, cvc-explicitTimezone-valid (¬ß4.3.14).
- Ratchet: unchanged (zero dateTimeStamp cases in the suite; regex widening is inert).
- Gate: build/test/vet/golangci-lint/conformance all green.
- Verdicts (chronicler addendum, recorded at land time ‚Äî mason wrote the entry
  above BEFORE the arbiter ruled): Arbiter round 1 on `wip/issue-122` **REJECT**
  (comment 4997317749), two doc-only findings, no logic defect: (1) the fail-open
  gap in conformance/datatypes.go lacked a greppable `GAP(datatypes)` token so it
  could not be inventoried alongside the other fail-open sites; (2) a
  datetimestamp_test.go docstring mis-attributed which enforcement path (facet
  cohort vs Parse-only) rejects the tz-absent case. Mason repair round (commit
  `26a5dfe`) added the `// GAP(datatypes)` marker and corrected the docstring;
  no code behaviour changed. Arbiter round 2 **ACCEPT** (comment 4997332999).

  `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` confirmed ratchet unchanged in both ‚Äî zero
  msData/datatypes/dateTimeStampNNN.xml cases in the current W3C checkout, so the
  lexical-cohort regex widening is inert today (no lane moved, no expectations
  file touched).
- Next (deferred, for cartographer post-land harvest): (1) file a tracking issue
  for the documented fail-open `GAP(datatypes)` in conformance/datatypes.go ‚Äî
  dateTimeStamp's Parse-only lexical-cohort path (execLexicalCase ‚Üí parseDateTime)
  does NOT enforce explicitTimezone=required, so a future tz-absent case would be
  false-ACCEPTED and must move to the facet cohort instead; harmless while zero

  precisionDecimal-family gaps. (2) NARROW-PRECEDENT caution (warden's explicit
  note): do NOT reflexively alias the next derived types
  (yearMonthDuration ¬ß3.4.26 / dayTimeDuration ¬ß3.4.27) onto duration the way

  defect (missing `xsi:noNamespaceSchemaLocation`) is a W3C test-suite bug, not
  ours ‚Äî worth a one-line note if this project ever tracks known-suite-defects,
  otherwise no action needed (it stays pinned `fail`, not a regression risk).
  No other deferred items ‚Äî clean single-round accept, no repair round, no
  residual gaps beyond the honest suite-file decline noted above.

## 2026-07-17 ‚Äî #124 widen datatypes Facets cohort to anyURI/hexBinary/base64Binary (mason)

- Widened the `datatypes` lane's Facets cohort (`conformance/datatypes.go`) to the
  three strict-mapped primitives `anyURI`, `hexBinary`, `base64Binary` by adding
  them to `facetsBaseTypes` (the `|`-alternation feeding both the directory and the
  filename-prefix of `facetsCase`). Zero backend change: all three are primitives
  strict already maps (#82 anyURI, #83 hexBinary/base64Binary), so `strictGoverns`
  resolves at the first step and validation runs through the existing generic
  pipeline (`value.ValidateLexical`).
- Spec (grounding on the issue, GROUNDING comment 4997679586): all three admit
  length/minLength/maxLength/pattern/enumeration (cos-applicable-facets ¬ß4.1.5,
  identical to string; unordered so NO bound facets), all already in `facetKinds`.
  The length UNIT split (¬ß4.3.1.3 clauses 1.1/1.2) ‚Äî characters for anyURI, decoded
  OCTETS for the binary types ‚Äî is already realized by `value.Lengthed` Len()
  dispatch: `anyURIVal.Len()` counts runes, `hexBinaryVal`/`base64BinaryVal.Len()`
  count decoded `[]byte`. Verified by reading `builtin/strict/anyuri.go` and
  `builtin/strict/binary.go`; no fix needed there. Rules exercised unchanged:
  cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4, cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4, cvc-enumeration-valid
  ¬ß4.3.5.4, cvc-length/minLength/maxLength-valid ¬ß4.3.1.3‚Äì4.3.3.3.
- One shape correction beyond the raw widening: the anyURI Facets dir carries
  out-of-cohort `anyURI_a*`/`anyURI_b*` cases that also match the filename regex.
  The `a*` cases already declined (value in an xsi:schemaLocation-qualified <bar>,
  not noNamespaceSchemaLocation). The `b*` cases carry zero <foo> (b001, values in
  repeated <bar>) or several <foo> (b006, a list-style multi-value instance), which
  the previous single `Foo fooElem` reader mis-read as an empty / last-wins value ‚Äî
  coincidentally PASSING b001/b005/b006 for the wrong reason. Changed
  `facetsInstance.Foo` to `Foos []fooElem` and made `readFacetsCase` require
  EXACTLY ONE <foo>, so every out-of-cohort anyURI shape is honestly declined
  (Fail, a recorded gap) rather than baking a wrong-reason pass into the ratchet.
  Confirmed via a throwaway DIAG-gated diagnostic (since deleted) that the exactly-
  one guard declines all 8 anyURI a*/b* instances and leaves every canonical
  <test><foo> case agreeing with the suite; non-ratchet `TestConformance` shows no
  regression from the guard.
- Observed locally (non-authoritative, no `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` ‚Äî arbiter-only): of the
  49 claimed Facets cases across the three dirs, 40 canonical-shape cases agree with
  the suite in both polarities (22 valid-expected, 18 invalid-expected), 8 anyURI
  out-of-cohort shapes decline (honest gaps), and 1 anyURI case (a schema-only
  entry) is unclaimed. Expected ratchet movement: datatypes lane up by the ~40
  agreeing New cases recorded `pass`, the ~8 anyURI gaps recorded `fail`; nothing
  flips downward; no other lane touched. Arbiter to confirm exact numbers.
- Tests (`conformance/datatypes_test.go`): added `TestDatatypesFacetsBinaryAndURI`
  (both polarities over real anyURI/hexBinary/base64Binary cases, with
  hexBinary_maxLength001 "abcdef"=3 octets and base64Binary_length002 "MS0yLTM="=5
  octets chosen so a regression to lexical-character counting would flip them, plus
  a wrong-expectation-must-Fail that is octet-unit-load-bearing) and
  `TestDatatypesFacetsShapeGuard` (readFacetsCase accepts the single-<foo> shape,
  declines b001 zero-<foo> and b006 multi-<foo>). Extended
  `TestDatatypesSelectorClaimsOnlyCohort` with one claim per new dir.
- Doc comments updated: facet-cohort header (#57 line adds #124), the claimed-base
  narrative, `facetsBaseTypes` doc (new types + length-unit paragraph), the
  `newDatatypesExec` cohort enumeration, `facetsInstance`'s shape note, and the

- Gate green: build, `go test ./...`, `go vet ./...`, `golangci-lint run`
  (0 issues), non-ratchet conformance. Did NOT run GOXSD_RATCHET=1 (arbiter-only).
- Verdicts (chronicler addendum, recorded at land time ‚Äî mason wrote the entry
  above BEFORE the arbiter ruled): Arbiter round 1 on `wip/issue-124` **ACCEPT**,

## 2026-07-17 ‚Äî issue #130 ‚Äî QName/NOTATION length-facet clause-1.3 exemption

- Shipped (mason): `value.lengthFacet.CheckValue` now short-circuits to accept
  ANY value when the type's `{primitive type definition}` is QName or NOTATION,
  per clause 1.3 of cvc-length-valid (¬ß4.3.1.3) / cvc-minLength-valid (¬ß4.3.2.3)
  / cvc-maxLength-valid (¬ß4.3.3.3) ‚Äî an unconditional "any {value} is
  facet-valid" no-op, independent of the bound and of `Lengthed.Len()`. Added
  unexported `lengthExemptPrimitive(st)` keying off the atomic `{variety}`'s
  `Primitive.Name()` (not the value's Go type, not a blanket is-atomic test ‚Äî the
  list case, clause 2, has no such exemption), the two builtin-name vars
  `qnameName`/`notationName`, and an `exempt bool` field on `lengthFacet` set at
  construction; `newLengthFacet` now takes `st *xsd.SimpleType` and the one
  `compile()` call site threads it through (mirrors newBoundFacet/newEnumFacet).
- Prior bug was a latent WRONG-REJECT (fail-closed polarity): a QName/NOTATION
  value under a length facet would have gated on `qnameVal.Len()`'s documented
  non-gating local-part rune count. Currently unreachable by the conformance
  suite (no selector routes a length facet at a QName/NOTATION value yet), so
  pure prerequisite cleanup ‚Äî ratchet UNCHANGED, expectations untouched.
- Tests: `TestLengthFacetsQNameNotationExempt` (builtin/strict, package strict)
  drives real QName and NOTATION values end-to-end through ValidateLexical under
  length=3/minLength=6/maxLength=2 bounds a 5-rune local part violates ‚Äî all
  accepted; plus narrow `value.TestLengthExemptPrimitive` covering primitive,
  QName restriction, string (not exempt), and nil-variety anySimpleType (no
  panic). Mutation-checked: removing the short-circuit fails both suites.
- Surface: none (predicate, vars, and struct field all unexported). Full gate
  (build/test/vet/golangci-lint 0 issues) + non-ratchet conformance green.
- Friction: (1) a mid-task `git checkout value/facets.go` (run to undo a mutation
  probe) silently reverted the unstaged implementation; caught by re-reading and
  re-applied. Lesson: never `git checkout` a file holding unstaged work ‚Äî restore
  the mutation with a targeted Edit instead. (2) mason authored the four bullets
  above INTO `docs/LOG/2026-07.md` in the implementation commit (`0911a67`) ‚Äî
  writing the log is the chronicler's Land-step duty, not mason's. The arbiter
  flagged it as a non-blocking process finding for the chronicler to reconcile
  (see below); this entry keeps mason's accurate content and adds the missing
  chronicler sections rather than rewriting. Recorded factually; no session was
  blocked, but the role boundary was crossed.
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` left zero diff under
  `conformance/testdata/expectations/`, working tree clean, no stray root files
  (arbiter-verified; copied from verdict, not recomputed). No selector routes a
  length facet at a QName/NOTATION value yet, so clause 1.3 is unreachable by the
  suite today ‚Äî pure prerequisite cleanup, no lane moved.
- Verdicts (chronicler addendum, recorded at Land ‚Äî mason wrote the four bullets
  above BEFORE the arbiter ruled): Arbiter round 1 on `wip/issue-130` **ACCEPT**
  (comment 4999660811), single round, no repair needed. Independently verified
  against `docs/specs/md/xmlschema11-2.md`: ¬ß4.3.1.3/¬ß4.3.2.3/¬ß4.3.3.3 clause 1.3
  read directly ‚Äî under clause 1 (`{variety}` atomic) the 1.1/1.2/1.3 sub-clauses
  are a mutually exclusive case split on `{primitive type definition}`, and 1.3
  ("if QName or NOTATION, then any {value} is facet-valid") is an unconditional
  no-op; clause 2 (list) carries no exemption, so the fix's keying off the atomic
  variety's resolved `Primitive.Name()` correctly covers a QName restriction and
  correctly excludes list-of-QName. Confirmed the short-circuit sits BEFORE the
  `Lengthed` assertion/panic, no schema-construction-time rejection was added, and

## 2026-07-17 ‚Äî issue #146 ‚Äî datatypes `<item ATTR=‚Ä¶>` lexical sub-shape routed (5 fail‚Üípass)

- Shipped: the datatypes lane now decodes the `<data><item SOMITEM_DATATYPE_X="v"/></data>`
  instance shape (commit `dd193c5`, mason), which carries no in-document
  `xsi:noNamespaceSchemaLocation` ‚Äî its schema is the shared sibling fixture
  `testdata/xsdtests/msData/datatypes/datatypes.xsd`, which types each
  `SOMITEM_DATATYPE_*` attribute directly as a facet-less builtin primitive.
  The lane's existing `readLexicalCase` only decoded the comp_foo/simpleTest
  shape, so these cases never reached the lexical check. Added a fallback path in
  `conformance/datatypes.go` (`execItemCase`/`readItemCase`/`decodeItemAttrTypes`)
  that parses the sibling `datatypes.xsd` (not hand-typed) into an attr‚Üíprimitive
  map and ANDs `parseOK` across every tested attribute per item, reusing the
  existing `sym`/`backend.Mapping` guards. `TestDatatypesLexicalItemShape` added
  in `conformance/datatypes_test.go`.
- Grounding (oracle, GROUNDING comment on #146): confirmed via
  docs/specs/md/xmlschema11-2.md that all five routed literals are genuinely
  lexically invalid ‚Äî durations `"P"` / `"P1Y2M3DT"` / `"P1"`
  (durationLexicalRep ¬ß3.3.6.2), `--02-30` / `--02-31`
  (con-gMonthDay-dayValue / con-gMonthDay-day ¬ß3.3.12.1-2),
  `+2001-07-11T12:23:45` (dateTimeLexicalRep ¬ß3.3.7.2), `+2001-07-11`
  (dateLexicalRep ¬ß3.3.9.2), all under cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4 ‚Äî and that
  `builtin/strict.New()` already rejects all five correctly. So this was a pure
  conformance-HARNESS routing gap, NOT a library correctness bug; no library code
  changed.
- Ratchet (arbiter, commit `41397c6`, ACCEPT): **datatypes lane 939‚Üí944 pass,
  25‚Üí20 fail** (964 total unchanged) ‚Äî exactly the 5 target cases flipped
  fail‚Üípass, nothing else moved, nothing regressed or vanished. Figures copied
  from the arbiter verdict, not recomputed. Full gate green (build/test/vet/lint,
  non-ratchet conformance); exported surface none (matches the issue's `## Surface`);
  blast radius verified as exactly these 5 files.
- Dismissed (no code change, both honest declines):
  - `string_pattern002_1031.i` ‚Äî an `xsd:list`-variety case; list/union varieties
    stay out of scope until #75 (rescoped to the list/union-variety Facets half).
    One traceability clause naming it was added to the existing "Still deferred"
    doc comment.

    fixture is missing `xsi:noNamespaceSchemaLocation`); unchanged.

## 2026-07-17 ‚Äî issue #131 ‚Äî QName/NOTATION lexical cohort claimed (mason, pre-arbiter)

- Shipped (branch `wip/issue-131`, not yet arbiter-judged at time of writing):
  a namespace-context adapter in the `conformance` package so the datatypes
  lexical cohort can decide the context-dependent QName/NOTATION primitive family.
  Surface: none (test-only, package `conformance`). No new `value` package surface
  needed ‚Äî `conformance` implements `value.Context` itself with an internal
  `nsContext` type, exactly as the issue anticipated.
- What was built: `execLexicalCase` now routes QName/NOTATION (isContextDependent)
  to `execContextualCase`, which reads each comp_foo/simpleTest literal WITH the
  in-scope XML namespace bindings via `readQNameContexts` ‚Äî a streaming
  `xml.Decoder` pass that tracks `xmlns:*`/`xmlns` declarations down the ancestor
  chain and snapshots them per leaf (a raw literal's prefix is character content,
  not an XML name the decoder resolves, so the accumulation is done by hand). The
  snapshot is wrapped in `nsContext`, which also binds the reserved prefixes
  `xml`/`xmlns` by definition (Namespaces in XML ¬ß3) and resolves the empty prefix
  to the default namespace (or no namespace when undeclared). `parseOK` gained a
  `ctx` param; the context-free primitives keep passing `nil`.
- Spec: cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4 (every rejection), QName lexical mapping ¬ß3.3.18,
  NOTATION ¬ß3.3.19 (mapping "as given for QName"). PRINCIPLES 19 (unbound prefix ‚áí
  real rejection, never a fabricated namespace).
- Cohort: QName is the whole exercised cohort today ‚Äî 11 cases
  (`QName001..011.xml`), all decided correctly in both polarities (4 valid:
  002/003/006/009; 7 invalid: 001/004/005/007/008/010/011). Key subtlety: QName009
  `xmlns:xsi` is suite-VALID because the reserved `xmlns` prefix is bound by
  definition ‚Äî the adapter binds it, so the case passes for the right reason, not
  by luck. NOTATION has ZERO plain lexical cases in the checkout (all its cases are
  facet-cohort under `Facets/NOTATION`), so it is listed in the regex for
  spec/mechanism parity and unexercised today.
- Expected ratchet: datatypes lane +11 pass (11 New QName cases), nothing flips
  downward. The QName cases also remain `fail` in the instance lane (stubFail,
  unchanged) ‚Äî the two lanes both list them, matching the established boolean/
  decimal pattern, so no vanish. Arbiter to confirm via `GOXSD_RATCHET=1`.
- Gate: `go build ./... && go test ./... && go vet ./...` green; `golangci-lint run`
  0 issues; read-only `go test ./conformance -run TestConformance` reports no
  regressions. New tests: `TestDatatypesLexicalQNameCohort` (11 cases + wrong-
  expectation Fail + adapter read-back) and `TestNSContextLookup` (prefix
  resolution unit test); `TestDatatypesSelectorClaimsOnlyCohort` extended.
- Facets over QName/NOTATION remain deferred (need the length clause-1.3 exemption
  and tuple enumeration) ‚Äî recorded in the "Still deferred" doc comment.

## 2026-07-17 ‚Äî issue #131 ‚Äî repair: exclude xmlns from resolvable QName prefixes (mason)
- Arbiter rejection (one finding): the pre-arbiter commit `4c31e50` had QName009
  (`xmlns:xsi`) inverted ‚Äî claimed suite-VALID because the adapter bound `xmlns`.
  Ground truth: `QName009_2092` in `DataTypes_w3c.xml` carries `validity="invalid"`
  (WG 2010-02-05 telcon, bugzilla 4053: no binding exists for `xmlns` as a prefix).
  The `.v` in the file name is an MS artifact; `resolveExpected` reads the catalog's
  real invalid value.
- Fix: dropped the `case "xmlns"` branch and the `xmlnsPrefixNS` constant from
  `nsContext.LookupNamespace`; only `xml` remains an implicitly-bound reserved
  prefix (Namespaces in XML ¬ß3). `xmlns` now returns `ok=false`, so strict's Parse
  rejects `xmlns:xsi` via cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4 ‚Äî matching the suite.

  QName009 ‚Üí invalid; `TestNSContextLookup` `xmlns` ‚Üí `("", false)`. Three doc

  now decide correctly in both polarities (valid: 002/003/006; invalid: 001/004/005/

## 2026-07-18 ‚Äî issue #125 ‚Äî datatypes Facets cohort admits QName (11 fail‚Üípass)

  real `value.Context` (built from the instance root's xmlns bindings via the
  existing `nsContext`/`childBindings` machinery from #131) into
  `execFacetsCase`'s `ValidateLexical` call, replacing the hardcoded `nil`
  (required even for the unprefixed QName literals ‚Äî `resolveQNameLexical`
  rejects a nil context unconditionally). Commits `7ecd4e1` (mason) + `e6d667c`
  (ratchet-recorded expectations).
- Grounding (oracle, GROUNDING comment): corrected this issue's own "Spec" text
  ‚Äî length/minLength/maxLength ARE applicable to QName/NOTATION per ¬ß4.1.5
  `cos-applicable-facets`, but vacuously pass per ¬ß4.3.1.3/¬ß4.3.2.3/¬ß4.3.3.3
  clause 1.3 (deprecated-but-legal), already correctly realized by #130's
  `lengthFacet` exemption and untouched here. So this was a harness-widening
  change, not a library correctness fix.
- Ratchet (arbiter ACCEPT, HEAD `7ecd4e1`, figures copied not recomputed):
  **datatypes lane 955‚Üí966 pass, 20‚Üí24 fail** (975‚Üí990 total). The +15 lines
  the ratchet wrote to `datatypes.txt` are exactly **11 pass** (length√ó3,
  maxLength√ó3, minLength√ó4, pattern√ó1) plus **4 honest fail-gaps**
  (enumeration001-004). Nothing regressed or vanished; no other lane's file
  touched. Arbiter independently confirmed the passes are genuine (reverted the
  length exemption, watched `foofo` flip to reject) and the enumeration declines
  are real gaps, not mis-decisions.
- Two deliberate, documented scope carve-outs (declined, not silently skipped):
  (a) QName `enumeration` cases are explicitly declined in `buildOwnFacets` ‚Äî
  `value.newEnumFacet` hardcodes a nil context when parsing enum member
  lexicals, which cannot resolve a schema-declared prefix like `foo:fo`; fixing
  it needs new `xsd.Facet`/`EffectiveFacet` surface + a warden pre-flight,
  beyond this "Surface: none" issue. (b) `NOTATION` was not added to
  `facetsBaseTypes` at all ‚Äî its Facets fixtures use an incompatible two-step
  restriction through a locally-named simpleType with `<xsd:notation>`
  declarations and the tested value carried in an attribute, which the cohort
  executor does not model.
- Gate: build/test/vet/lint green; read-only conformance no regressions;
  `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` exit 0. No new exported surface.
- Next: file the two follow-ups the arbiter flagged for the post-land harvest ‚Äî
  (a) QName/NOTATION enumeration-facet schema-declaring-context threading (a
  `value`/`xsd` design item mirroring #131's lexical-cohort fix, one level up

## 2026-07-18 ‚Äî #134 ‚Äî datatypes lane: removed redundant fallbackPrimitives shim

- Removed the `fallbackPrimitives` type + its `Mapping` method and the
  `value.Override(fallbackPrimitives{}, strict.New())` composition in
  `conformance/datatypes.go`; `builtin.Seed` is now fed `strict.New()` directly.
  Post-#115 strict maps all 20 builtin primitives (19 spec-mandatory of
  Datatypes ¬ß3.3 + precisionDecimal), so the no-op identity fallback was fully
  redundant. It was also the wrong polarity as a floor: an accept-everything
  identity `Parse` would MASK a silently-dropped strict mapping by accepting
  every lexical, whereas `builtin.Seed`'s own precondition scan fails loud with
  a typed `*builtin.MissingPrimitivesError`. Net: a latent fail-open mask
  converted to the fail-loud behavior Seed already provides.
- Collapsed the now-identical `backend`/`strictBackend` pair to a single strict
  backend; `execFacetsCase` drops its second backend parameter. Refreshed the
  `newDatatypesExec`, `execFacetsCase`, and `strictGoverns` doc comments to drop
  stale fallback/Override prose. Updated both `value.Override(...)` sites in
  `datatypes_test.go` (TestDatatypesBackendSeeds still guards the precondition,
  now against `strict.New()` directly).
- Spec: n/a (test-harness cleanup; builtin.Seed's primitive-coverage
  precondition, xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß3.3 structurally).
- Ratchet: unchanged.
- Gate: go build/test/vet + golangci-lint (0 issues) + conformance
  (TestConformance) all green (mason-run; arbiter to re-verify).

## 2026-07-18 ‚Äî #135 ‚Äî conformance: claim the Saxon precisionDecimal instance cohort

- Widened the `datatypes` lane to claim and decide the Saxon precisionDecimal
  instance cases under `saxonData/PDecimal/pdecimalNNN.{vK,nK}.xml`. These were
  UNDISCOVERED, not merely unclaimed: the W3C suite moved the precisionDecimal
  sets out of `suite.xml` (withdrawn from XSD 1.1, retained as a WG Note) into
  `extra-suite.xml`, which discovery never read. So `runner.go` now discovers
  `suite.xml` AND its sibling `extra-suite.xml`, de-duplicating the one shared
  set (`common/introspection.testSet`, listed in both) by resolved path
  (`casesFromIndex`/`seenSets`) so it is not a spurious duplicate-ID error.
- New `execPDecimalCase`/`readPDecimalCase` decode the cohort's distinct shape (a
  `<doc>` root with repeated `<e value="‚Ä¶"/>` children, all validated against ONE
  type; schema out-of-band, derived from the case-prefix filename ‚Üí sibling
  `pdecimalNNN.xsd`). The tested leaf is synthesized (precisionDecimal primitive +
  schema facets) and run through the existing `value.ValidateLexical` pipeline ‚Äî
  no new value code. Added `FacetMaxScale`/`FacetMinScale` to the lane's
  `facetKinds` (precisionDecimal-only, harmless to the msData cohort).
- Spec-correct facet behavior falls out of the existing pipeline: totalDigits
  vacuously passes zero+specials (value.TotalDigits‚Üí1, xsd-precisionDecimal.md
  ¬ß4.1, distinct from decimal); NaN fails EVERY bound facet over the partial order
  (boundFacet incomparable‚áíreject, ¬ß3.1/¬ß4.3.7‚Äì4.3.10); maxScale/minScale skip the
  specials' absent ¬∑scale¬∑ (#133); enumeration is value-space equal-or-identical on
  ¬∑numericalValue¬∑ (10 == 1.0E1; NaN matches a NaN member by identity, ¬ß4.3.5.4).
- Scope: only the directly-mapped and single-step restriction cases (pdecimal001‚Äì
  008,010) are decided. The two-step chain (016), list (019) and union (020) shapes
  are DECLINED by `decodePDecimalSchema` (honest gaps, Fail). One suite quirk kept
  spec-correct rather than bent: pdecimal006.n2 ("NaN" vs a NaN-bearing enumeration)
  is spec-VALID (identity match) but suite-declared invalid, so it records a Fail
  against the suite ‚Äî flagged in `execPDecimalCase`, per the #135 GROUNDING. The
  arbiter independently confirmed this via `GOXSD_CASE` (goxsd8 computes VALID) and
  UPHELD it as spec-correct ‚Äî cvc-enumeration-valid ¬ß4.3.5.4 "equal or identical"
  plus xsd-precisionDecimal.md ¬ß3.1's single NaN value identical to itself ‚Äî an
  honest goxsd8-vs-suite disagreement, not a false-accept and not a mason error.
- Deferred: the IBM `ibmData/D3_3_4` precisionDecimal shape (several named types per
  schema) is NOT claimed ‚Äî a distinct, larger executor; its instance cases route to
  the inert `instance` lane as recorded gaps meanwhile. Follow-up issue candidate.
- Spec: cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4, cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4, cvc-enumeration-valid
  ¬ß4.3.5.4, cvc-totalDigits-valid (xsd-precisionDecimal.md ¬ß4.1), cvc-min/maxInclusive/
  Exclusive-valid ¬ß4.3.7‚Äì4.3.10, cvc-maxScale-valid ¬ß4.2.3, cvc-minScale-valid ¬ß4.3.3.
- Ratchet (arbiter-recorded via `GOXSD_RATCHET=1`; ACCEPT on commit `74a84b9`,
  parent `b476b21` = origin/main): datatypes lane +50 new cases ‚Äî 40 pass
  (pdecimal001‚Äì008,010 both polarities) + 10 honest gaps (016/019/020 declines and
  the 006.n2 suite quirk); instance lane +69, schema lane +54, all newly-discovered
  precisionDecimal schema / D3_3_4 cases entering as New gaps. ZERO deletions and no
  downward flip in any lane; xpath/json/ber untouched (0 cases). Per-lane numstat
  50/0, 69/0, 54/0.

## 2026-07-18 ‚Äî issue #141 ‚Äî yearMonthDuration/dayTimeDuration mapped

- Shipped: builtin/strict now maps xs:yearMonthDuration (¬ß3.4.26) and
  xs:dayTimeDuration (¬ß3.4.27) into backend.Mapping, so both validate through
  value.ValidateLexical. New files yearmonthduration.go / daytimeduration.go +
  two strict.go case arms; neither aliases parseDuration/canonicalDuration.
- Design (oracle GROUNDING + warden PRE-FLIGHT on #141): each type gets its OWN
  anchored lexical regex gating the narrower space (parseDuration's wide ¬ß3.3.6.2
  grammar would false-accept a cross-half literal ‚Äî value.Mapping.Parse contract).
  Parse reuses duration's durationFields extraction and addMonths/addSeconds/
  addSecondFraction math verbatim; the non-applicable half is a hard `new(big.Int)`
  / `new(big.Rat)` stated at the construction site (definitionally absent, not
  coincidentally zero ‚Äî STYLE D3), not laundered through helpers on empty groups.
- Canonical: dayTimeDuration reuses durationVal.Canonical (¬∑months¬∑ always 0 ‚áí
  default day-time branch, whose "T0S" zero case is inside [^YM]*(T.*)?).
  yearMonthDuration CANNOT ‚Äî its ¬∑months¬∑=0 value has NO canonical representation
  (¬ß3.4.26.1 Note: duration's "PT0S" is outside [^DT]*), surfaced as a PLAIN
  fmt.Errorf wrapping an unexported errNoYearMonthCanonical sentinel ‚Äî NOT an
  xsderr verdict, because the zero value is a legally VALID value, not a violation
  (per warden refinement #2, xsderr.Error contract).
- Spec: cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4 (Parse rejections cite ¬ß3.4.26.1/¬ß3.4.27.1);
  cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4 (seeded fixed pattern [^DT]* / [^YM]*(T.*)?);
  ¬ß3.4.26.1/¬ß3.4.27.1 lexical + canonical mapping; ¬ß2.3.1 dt-canonical-mapping
  "(where possible)" partial-domain license. No gen_typespec.go work ‚Äî the fixed
  facet tables were already generated correctly.
- Tests: parse/canonical round-trip tables per type; cross-half + grammar-trap
  rejection tables (cvc-datatype-valid); yearMonthDuration zero-value no-canonical
  case (Parse accepts "P0Y"/"P0M", Canonical returns a non-verdict error);
  #122-shaped seeded-type value.ValidateLexical tests proving the fixed pattern
  facet reaches enforcement in both polarities (year-month accepted / rejected as
  cvc-pattern-valid mirror for the other type). Added a `seededType` helper.
- Ratchet: unchanged (arbiter runs it). No corpus regression; new capability +
  latent-correctness (independent lexical-space gate + zero-value handling).

## 2026-07-18 ‚Äî issue #149 ‚Äî LOG entry (not lane-file comment) is the dismissal record

- Shipped (e1dd769): conformance/testdata/expectations/README.md gains a 9-line
  paragraph establishing that the durable dismissal record for an honestly-declined
  recorded `fail` case is the docs/LOG entry (and/or a GitHub tracking-issue
  comment) ‚Äî NOT a `#` comment in the lane file. Doc-only; no Go/test/expectations
  changes.
- Why: WriteExpectations (conformance/expectations.go:190) regenerates each lane
  file purely from its in-memory status map on every ratchet run, with no
  comment-emission channel ‚Äî so any hand-added `#` comment in a lane file is
  silently discarded on the next write. Some past triage issues (e.g. #146) asked
  for the incompatible file-comment pattern; #149 was filed to resolve that standing
  contradiction by naming the one place a dismissal actually survives.
- Verified: arbiter confirmed the factual claim against the actual WriteExpectations
  implementation before ACCEPT.
- Arbiter: ACCEPT, no findings. Gate green ‚Äî go build/test/vet, golangci-lint (0
  issues).
- Ratchet: unchanged (doc-only; lane files untouched).
- Next: arbiter-accepted; orchestrator checkpoints/lands #149.

## 2026-07-18 ‚Äî issue #152 ‚Äî thread schema-declaring namespace context into QName/NOTATION enumeration facets

- Problem: `value.newEnumFacet` parsed every enumeration `{value}` member with a
  hardcoded `nil` context, so a prefixed QName/NOTATION member ("foo:fo") could not
  resolve its prefix. The four W3C `Facets/QName/QName_enumeration001-004` cases
  were declined in `buildOwnFacets` (an honest #125 gap) rather than decided.
- Shape (warden-ruled, implemented exactly): namespace context lives PER MEMBER,
  not per Facet. New exported surface in `xsd`: `EnumerationMember` (Lexical /
  NamespaceBindings / DefaultNamespace, immutable, `NewEnumerationMember` with the
  `*string` absence discipline ‚Äî no baseURI per warden), `NewEnumerationFacet`
  (mirrors `NewAssertionsFacet`), and `Facet.EnumerationMembers()` (mirrors
  `Facet.Assertions()`). `NewFacet` now PANICS on `FacetEnumeration` (as it does for
  `FacetAssertions`); `Facet.Values()` DERIVES the lexical strings from the members
  (STYLE D3, no double storage). `EffectiveFacet` unchanged (replace-kind overlay
  carries members through, warden-confirmed).
- `value`: unexported per-member `memberContext` adapter (¬ß3.3.18 reserved-prefix
  rules matched to `conformance.nsContext` exactly ‚Äî `xml` bound, `xmlns` never,
  empty prefix ‚Üí default). `newEnumFacet` iterates members, builds the adapter, and
  remaps a failed member `Parse` to `src-enumeration-value` (¬ß4.3.5.3, the
  `src-pattern-value` sibling ‚Äî already in the xsderr catalog).
- `conformance`: `decodeRestriction` now snapshots each `<enumeration>`'s in-scope
  bindings down the schema document's ancestor chain (schema-side analogue of #131's
  instance-side `readQNameContexts`); `buildOwnFacets` retires the #125 QName-enum
  decline and threads the snapshot into `xsd.NewEnumerationMember`.
- Cohort: QName_enumeration001/003 (empty instance value ‚Üí invalid) and 002/004
  ("foo:fo" resolving to the same expanded QName as the schema member ‚Üí valid) all
  decide correctly in both polarities (driven end-to-end + flipped-expectation in
  `TestDatatypesQNameFacets`). Spec: cvc-enumeration-valid ¬ß4.3.5.4,
  src-enumeration-value ¬ß4.3.5.3, dt-QName ¬ß3.3.18, st-restrict-facets ¬ß3.16.6.4.
- Ratchet: strict `datatypes` lane +4 (QName_enumeration001-004 fail‚Üípass);
  arbiter records via GOXSD_RATCHET (mason does not run it). Gate green: go
  build/test/vet, golangci-lint 0 issues.
- Next: arbiter review of the diff (incl. separate warden diff review of the new
  exported surface); land on ACCEPT.
- Post-land pass (2026-07-18, PR #186 squash `b59e833`): unblock scan found no
  issue with a hard `Depends on #152`; #153 (NOTATION Facets shape) carries only a
  soft co-requisite cross-reference and stays `ready` (no relabel) ‚Äî commented there
  that #152's landed surface now backs its enumeration slice. Harvest: the warden
  diff review's three non-blocking notes (xml-namespace URI triplicated across the
  pure-leaf/no-import-conformance boundary, `memberContext`/`nsContext` duplication,
  `NewEnumerationFacet(nil)` representable-but-unreachable) were all explicit
  dispositions ("no action required to land" / "accepted as consistent"), not
  deferred follow-ups ‚Äî nothing filed. `src-*-value` remap precedent checked: the
  spec defines an SRC-value rule only for `pattern` and `enumeration` (both now
  remapped); `newBoundFacet`'s bare `cvc-datatype-valid` propagation is correct as
  there is no precise `src-*` target for bound facet values. No new issues.

## 2026-07-19 ‚Äî issue #153 ‚Äî NOTATION Facets-cohort shape claimed

- Shipped (`9e6bd5c`): `conformance/datatypes.go` gains a bespoke reader+decoder+executor for
  the NOTATION Facets cohort ‚Äî `notationFacetsCase` selector (ORed into
  `selectsDatatypes`, new dispatch branch in `newDatatypesExec`),
  `decodeNotationRestriction` (single streaming pass that collects BOTH restriction
  steps instead of returning at the first `</restriction>` like `decodeRestriction`),
  `readNotationFacetsCase`, and `execNotationFacetsCase`. The generic
  `decodeRestriction`/`readFacetsCase`/`execFacetsCase` machinery is untouched
  (regression firewall ‚Äî same bespoke-pair precedent as #135/#146).
- Shape: each fixture is a two-step restriction ‚Äî named `buildNotation` restricts
  `xsd:NOTATION` with enums jpeg/mpeg/g (¬ß3.3.19 enumeration-required-notation),
  then an anonymous attribute simpleType restricts THAT with one tested facet;
  tested value in `<foo>`'s `attrTest` attribute. The executor synthesizes the
  two-level `xsd.SimpleType` chain (middle = NOTATION+enums, leaf = middle+tested
  facet) and decides via `value.ValidateLexical`, reusing `EffectiveFacets`'
  supersede overlay unchanged. The sibling `<xsd:notation>` decls are not
  load-bearing for any instance verdict (¬ß3.14.1 is a schema-time SCC) and are not
  parsed (STYLE D4).
- Cohort: all 15 `Facets/NOTATION/NOTATION_*.xml` cases now decide (harness diag +
  `TestDatatypesNotationFacets` end-to-end + flipped-expectation). enumeration001/003
  (empty attrTest vs non-empty leaf enum ‚Üí invalid) and every other case valid
  (length family vacuous per ¬ß4.3.1.3 clause 1.3; pattern001 matches; leaf enum
  supersedes middle's). Spec: cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4, cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4,
  cvc-enumeration-valid ¬ß4.3.5.4, st-restrict-facets ¬ß3.16.6.4.
- Ratchet: strict `datatypes` lane +15 ‚Äî 15 NEW rows decided at pass, not a
  fail‚Üípass transition: the lane's selector never claimed the
  `Facets/NOTATION/NOTATION_*.xml` cases before (`selectsDatatypes` returned false;
  the selector-claim test flips `NOTATION_enumeration001.xml` from unclaimed to
  claimed in this same change), so `NOTATION` was previously outside the ratchet's
  denominator entirely. Recorded by the arbiter via `GOXSD_RATCHET` in `5ee92da`
  (mason does not run it). Gate green: go build/test/vet, golangci-lint 0 issues.
- Next: arbiter ACCEPTed (verdict on #153); open the PR (`Closes #153`) and
  squash-merge, then a post-land unblock scan.

## 2026-07-19 ‚Äî issue #158 ‚Äî value: compile() fail-loud on unhandled FacetKind

- Shipped (`24810b3`): added a `default:` case to `compile()`'s FacetKind
  switch in `value/facets.go` that panics with
  `"value: compile: unhandled FacetKind %s"` instead of silently dropping the
  facet. Closes the silent-drop bug CLASS that #133 fixed only for its specific
  maxScale/minScale instance ‚Äî #133 added FacetMaxScale/FacetMinScale checkers
  but left the switch's no-default gap intact, so any FUTURE FacetKind added
  without a matching `compile()` arm would again be dropped with no signal.
  #158 converts that latent no-op into a caught failure at the next enum
  extension. Scope fully closed by this one change (no residual gap, unlike
  #133).
- Convention: panic (not `*xsderr.Error`) is deliberate and matches this file's
  kind-dispatch sites (`boundFacet.violates`/`boundRule`/`digitsRule`/
  `lengthRule`/`scaleRule`) and `ValidateLexical`'s panic doc ‚Äî a missing
  checker is a schema-construction / programmer error the caller must already
  have rejected, not an instance validity verdict.
- Test: new `TestCompileUnhandledFacetKindPanics` in `value/facets_test.go`
  forges an out-of-range `FacetKind(99)` as an own facet and asserts the panic
  fires; mutation-verified (removing the `default:` makes the test fail).
- Trade-off (accepted, documented in code comment + commit message): adding
  `default:` disables golangci-lint's `exhaustive` compile-time
  FacetKind-coverage check for this switch (`.golangci.yml` sets
  `default-signifies-exhaustive: true`). A future FacetKind addition is now
  caught at test/runtime via the panic instead of at lint time ‚Äî still strictly
  better than a silent no-op drop.
- Surface: none ‚Äî no new exported symbols.
- Spec: n/a (defensive kind-dispatch hardening; no spec rule newly
  implemented).
- Ratchet: unchanged ‚Äî defensive-only change, no behavior difference for the 16
  currently-handled FacetKinds. Arbiter confirmed via `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` with no
  expectation-file diffs.
- Verdict: arbiter ACCEPT. Gate green (go build/test/vet + golangci-lint +
  conformance).

## 2026-07-19 ‚Äî /retro Part 2: steward architecture audit

- Scope: import graph + exported surface vs ARCHITECTURE.md; duplicate
  concepts/representations (upkeep-judged); exported-symbol usage vs godoc;

  none was warranted.

  `xsderr` imports nothing from the module, `xsd` imports only `xsderr`,
  nothing imports `conformance`, no adapter decoder leaks into a non-adapter
  package. `parser/xmltree.Name` vs `xsd.QName` is the sanctioned deliberate

  no STYLE 8 removals.

  accretion (chronicler friction #2, issues #135/#146/#153):** intentional,
  justified isolation ‚Äî NOT a duplication problem. Each cohort triple decodes
  a distinct frozen W3C fixture shape and funnels semantics through shared
  library entry points; upkeep coupling is low; the separation is a
  regression firewall serving the one rule. Recorded as a steward ruling in
  ARCHITECTURE.md's "Conformance & ratchet" section so it is not re-flagged.

## 2026-07-19 ‚Äî #162 ‚Äî conformance: claim the IBM D3_3_4 precisionDecimal cohort (multi-type-per-schema executor)

- Widened the `datatypes` lane to decide the IBM `ibmData/{valid,instance_invalid}/
  D3_3_4/*` precisionDecimal cohort ‚Äî a SECOND, distinct shape from #135's
  single-leaf Saxon PDecimal cohort. Where #135 validated many `<e value="‚Ä¶"/>`
  children against ONE type, D3_3_4 schemas declare SEVERAL named precisionDecimal
  simpleTypes and route each instance element to its own matching type. New
  `execD34Case`/`readD34Case` + decoders (`decodeD34Instance`/`decodeD34Schema`/
  `indexD34Types`/`d34RootElemTypes`/`d34SchemaLocation`) and selector `d34Case`
  in `conformance/datatypes.go`; new test `TestDatatypesD34Cohort` in
  `conformance/datatypes_test.go`. Test-only, package `conformance` ‚Äî no library
  surface change, no new `xsderr` rule ID.
- Schema resolution differs deliberately from #135: the schema is read from the
  instance's own `xsi:schemaLocation` (namespace/location pair), NOT a
  case-prefix filename derivation ‚Äî the Saxon prefix-stripping trick does NOT
  hold here (e.g. `d3_3_4ii01a.xml` shares `d3_3_4ii01.xsd`, a different prefix).
- Decidable shape: index every named simpleType that is a DIRECT single-step
  `<restriction base="(prefix:)?precisionDecimal">`, and require the schema's
  `<element name="root">` to carry an INLINE `<complexType><sequence>` whose every
  child binds a `type=` attribute resolving into that index. The `type=` attribute
  is resolved per child ‚Äî never guessed from the element name (v14's
  `elMinMaxScale` binds `decMinMaxScale`, not a name-matched type). Decided:
  `d3_3_4v14`, `v23`, `v24` (valid) and `d3_3_4ii01[,a-f]`, `ii02`
  (instance_invalid). `ii01`'s Arabic-Indic-digit child `ŸÝŸ°Ÿ£` is a genuine INVALID
  verdict, not a decline.
- Honest declines (ok=false, recorded gap ‚Äî never a partial decision): v15 (root
  is a type-reference, no inline complexType), v16 (`<list>` variety), v17
  (`<union>` variety), v18 (children use `ref=` not `type=`), v19‚Äìv22 (3-step
  restriction chains ‚Äî same multi-step decline class as the Saxon cohort's
  `pdecimal016`).
- No new value/builtin/xsd code: reuses `strict.New()`'s precisionDecimal mapping
  (#115), `buildOwnFacets`, `xsd.NewSimpleType`, `value.ValidateLexical`,
  `strictGoverns`, `primitiveOfType`, `facetChild`, `synthNS` unchanged. Every
  rule ID is already implemented and merely re-exercised by the new
  reader/executor pair.
- Spec (all in place and reused unchanged): cvc-datatype-valid ¬ß4.1.4;
  cvc-pattern-valid ¬ß4.3.4.4; cvc-enumeration-valid ¬ß4.3.5.4 (value-space
  equal-or-identical; 10 == 1.0E1, NaN matches a NaN member by identity);
  cvc-min/maxInclusive/Exclusive-valid ¬ß4.3.7‚Äì4.3.10 (NaN incomparable ‚áí fails
  every bound, xsd-precisionDecimal.md ¬ß3.1); cvc-totalDigits-valid
  (xsd-precisionDecimal.md ¬ß4.1.1 ‚Äî zero + specials vacuous, NOT decimal's
  ¬ß4.3.11.3); cvc-maxScale-valid ¬ß4.2.3 / cvc-minScale-valid ¬ß4.3.3 (#133 ‚Äî zero
  is NOT scale-exempt unlike totalDigits, since ¬∑scale¬∑ is absent only for the
  three specials).
- Not reachable: `NaN.xml`/`NaN.xsd` in `ibmData/valid/D3_3_4/` are referenced by
  no testGroup in `ibmMeta/precisionDecimal.testSet`, so `parseSuite` never emits
  a case for them ‚Äî orphaned fixtures, absent from the discovered set. The 20
  `d3_3_4si09`‚Äì`si28` schema_invalid files are schemaTest-only (schema-construction
  invalidity), structurally excluded by `selectsDatatypes` (gates on
  `kind == kindInstance`), same as the Saxon cohort's schema-kind cases.
- Ratchet (arbiter-recorded via `GOXSD_RATCHET=1`; ACCEPT, commit `27983fc`,
  implementation `77e06db`, parent origin/main): ONLY `datatypes.txt` changed.
  datatypes lane +11 passes (`d3_3_4ii01[,a-f]`, `ii02`, `v14`, `v23`, `v24`) and
  +8 recorded-gap fails (`v15`‚Äì`v22`, honestly declined, New-at-fail). All 6 lanes
  reconciled: 0 regressed, 0 vanished. `instance.txt`/`schema.txt` untouched ‚Äî the
  declined instance cases stay `fail` in the overlapping `instance` lane exactly as
  the existing datatypes-lane instance cases already do (lateral move, established
  pattern, never a downward flip of a previously-passing case). Figures copied from
  the arbiter's verdict comment, not recomputed.
- Gate: arbiter re-verified ‚Äî `go build ./... && go vet ./... && go test ./...`
  green, `golangci-lint run` 0 issues, `go test ./conformance -run TestConformance`
  green (no regression), `TestDatatypesD34Cohort` PASS (asserts both polarities on
  decidable cases + declines on v15‚Äìv22). Verdict ACCEPT on #162.
- Friction / Next: mason again wrote an unauthorized `docs/LOG` entry inside its
  implementation commit (`77e06db`), reverted here in `5104bc2` so this single
  authoritative entry could be written at land. This is a REPEAT of the exact
  failure mode the 2026-07-19 second /retro flagged as a watch-item ("watch whether
  the mason.md boundary clause ends the mason-authored-LOG recurrence") ‚Äî it
  recurred on the very next issue, so the mason.md boundary clause alone is
  evidently NOT sufficient. Recording as a concrete recurrence data point for the

## 2026-07-19 ‚Äî #166 ‚Äî value: document per-value partial-domain Canonical error case (doc-only)

- Extended the doc comments on `value.Mapping.Canonical` (struct-level prose +
  field comment, `value/backend.go`) and `value.Canonical` (`value/value.go`,
  commit `c424173`) to document a previously-undocumented contract case: a
  NON-nil `Canonical` func may legitimately return a PLAIN (non-`*xsderr.Error`)
  error for one specific VALID value that has no canonical lexical form of its
  own ‚Äî the "per-value partial-domain" case ‚Äî distinct from the existing
  whole-type `Canonical == nil` case (e.g. QName). No signature, field, or
  behavior change; the two cases are kept textually distinct in the prose.
- Grounded (oracle GROUNDING, issue #166): dt-canonical-mapping ¬ß2.3.1's
  "(where possible)" domain hedge + the concrete in-codebase precedent
  `builtin/strict/yearmonthduration.go`'s `canonicalYearMonthDuration`, which
  returns a plain `fmt.Errorf` for the yearMonthDuration value where ¬∑months¬∑=0 ‚àß
  ¬∑seconds¬∑=0 ‚Äî duration's canonical "PT0S" falls outside yearMonthDuration's
  `[^DT]*` lexical space (¬ß3.4.26.1 Note). Also cites xmlschema11-1.md
  Appendix G.1.8 item 5.
- Spec: xmlschema11-2.md ¬ß2.3.1 (dt-canonical-mapping + Note), ¬ß3.4.26.1
  (yearMonthDuration Note); xmlschema11-1.md Appendix G.1.8 item 5. Doc-only,
  no rule ID newly implemented.
- Provenance: #166 harvested from #141's landing post-land pass (2026-07-18).
  Arbiter verdict ACCEPT (issue #166 verdict comment): prose verified verbatim
  against local specs, two cases kept distinct, no unauthorized docs/LOG touch in
  the mason commit, full gate green (build/test/vet/lint/conformance all pass).
- Ratchet: unchanged (doc-only; behavior untouched, `GOXSD_RATCHET` not run).

## 2026-07-19 ‚Äî #167 ‚Äî parser: raw XSD schema-document tree (parse phase)

- Shipped (commit `075d297`) the first slice of a new `parser` package: reading
  an XSD schema document into an internal element TREE (parent/child linkage) on
  top of the existing `parser/xmltree` streaming token reader. New files
  `parser/tree.go` (`Node` sealed sum, `*Element`, `*Text`) and
  `parser/document.go` (`Document`, `ReadDocument`, base-URI composition), with an
  external `parser_test` suite in `parser/document_test.go`. One export in the
  existing leaf package: `parser/xmltree`'s `xmlNamespaceURI` ‚Üí `XMLNamespaceURI`
  (`name.go`, `scope.go`). No `xsd` component production in this slice ‚Äî pure raw
  parse-phase infrastructure.
- Exported surface (minimal, each mapped to a named near-term consumer): `parser.Node`
  (sealed by unexported `node()`), `parser.Element` (Name/Attributes/LookupPrefix/
  Loc/Parent/Children/BaseURI ‚Äî all delegating to an unexported
  `src *xmltree.StartElement`, never re-derived), `parser.Text` (Data/Loc),
  `parser.Document` (URI/Root/IsSchema), `parser.ReadDocument(uri string, r io.Reader)
  (*Document, error)`, and `xmltree.XMLNamespaceURI`. No embedding, no exported
  struct fields, no re-exported `Offset()`.
- Grounded (oracle GROUNDING, issue #167): schema-document recognition at this raw
  layer is a purely NOMINAL check ‚Äî root expanded name == `{http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema}schema`
  (Glossary "schema document"; ¬ß3.17.2). Full sd-valid/S4S conformance (¬ß2.4) and
  ¬ß4.2.2 conditional-inclusion preprocessing are heavier LATER phases and must not
  happen here; `{target namespace}` interpretation (from the `targetNamespace`
  attribute per ¬ß3.17.2) is component-production, not namespace-scope tracking, so
  it does NOT belong at this layer. ¬ß3.3.18 (xmlschema11-2) makes per-node in-scope
  namespace bindings + parent linkage the load-bearing facts src-resolve (¬ß3.17.6.2)
  needs. Crucially: `xml:base` / base-URI composition is genuinely NOT defined in
  local Structures (zero "xml:base" hits) ‚Äî only named by reference (¬ß3.13.2,
  ¬ß4.3.2), deferred by xml-infoset.md to [[XML Base]] without reproducing the
  algorithm ‚Äî so it is implemented as EXTERNAL RFC 3986 knowledge
  (`net/url.URL.ResolveReference`) with a deliberate no-`src-*`/`cos-*`-citation
  rationale rather than a fabricated cite.
- Unusually thorough review chain ‚Äî three independent passes:
  - **Warden PRE-FLIGHT: REVISE** (before any code) ‚Äî 15 concrete shape corrections.
    Load-bearing ones: the tree must live in `parser`, NOT `parser/xmltree` (whose
    doc.go promises bounded memory / STYLE P4 ‚Äî a whole-document tree would violate
    it); reuse xmltree's Name/Attribute/Loc/scope machinery via an unexported
    delegate field (no embedding, no parallel `parser.QName`); collapse the node
    sealed sum (a tree needs no EndElement); retain character data as first-class
    `*Text` children with NO lossy concatenating `Text()` convenience (D3); and the
    hardest MUST-FIX ‚Äî `IsSchema()` must be a pure DERIVED predicate, never a stored
    bool and never a constructor error, since no spec rule exists for "not a schema
    document" at this layer and ¬ß3.17.2 says `<schema>` need not be the document
    element (a root-only reject would overreach).
  - **Warden DIFF REVIEW: APPROVE** (post-implementation, `075d297`) ‚Äî independently
    re-verified all 15 pre-flight points against the actual landed diff (not the
    mason's report); two soft non-blocking notes only.
  - **Arbiter VERDICT: ACCEPT** ‚Äî a third fully independent pass, not a rubber-stamp:
    personally re-derived the RFC 3986 base-URI arms by hand (inherit / relative-
    resolve `sub/` ‚Üí `.../base/sub/` / absolute-replace, each mutation-killable),
    re-confirmed `IsSchema()` never caches and never errors, and ran its OWN fresh
    `docs/LOG` boundary check ‚Äî `git diff --name-only` = exactly the 5 parser files,
    nothing under `docs/LOG/` (process issue #195's failure mode did not recur here).
- Spec: xmlschema11-1 ¬ß2.4, ¬ß3.13.2, ¬ß3.17.2, ¬ß3.17.6.2, ¬ß4.2.2, ¬ß4.3.2, Glossary
  "schema document"; xmlschema11-2 ¬ß3.3.18; xml-infoset "Base URIs" intro, ¬ß2.2
  properties 7/8. No new rule ID implemented (raw tree carries facts; validation is
  later). The xml:base composition rule is deliberately external, uncited.
- Gate: `go build/test/vet ./...` green (incl. `parser` and `parser/xmltree` after
  the rename), `golangci-lint run` 0 issues, `go test ./conformance -run TestConformance`
  clean read-only (no movement). Ratchet unchanged ‚Äî no conformance lane is wired to
  this slice yet, so `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` was correctly NOT run (nothing may move); the
  read-only run confirms no regression.
- Process: per the orchestrator, mason was explicitly instructed NOT to write a LOG
  entry this round (open process issue #195: mason recurring on unauthorized docs/LOG
  commits) ‚Äî the chronicler kept that responsibility. This single authoritative entry
  is being written at land, and mason's `075d297` touched no file under `docs/LOG/`
  (independently confirmed by both the warden diff review and the arbiter). A clean
  data point for #195: the boundary held this issue.
- Next: no `xsd` component production yet ‚Äî later parse-phase slices wire the loader/
  Resolver (phase 2, actual location resolution/fetching), ¬ß4.2.2 conditional-inclusion
  preprocessing, and src-resolve (¬ß3.17.6.2) walking parent links to a `<schema>`
  ancestor. A future slice may add the currently-defensive-only test for a malformed
  `xml:base` lexical that trips `composeBaseURI`'s `url.Parse` error path (the arbiter
  flagged it as an uncovered but correctly-wrapped branch, not a finding).
- Post-land pass (cartographer): no issue unblocked ‚Äî the only open issues naming #167
  are #174 (still `blocked` on #172/#173) and #176 (does not depend on #167); the five
  leaf follow-ups #72/#70/#63/#51/#46 point at the producer/finalize sub-slices, not
  #167. Progress-commented epic #79 (1/17 sub-slices; seam decisions recorded for the
  next M4 slice). No new issue filed: both warden soft notes were marked no-change, and
  the arbiter's untested-defensive-`url.Parse`-branch note is already captured in the
  "Next" bullet above as a future-touch-point (a producer slice will exercise `xml:base`
  naturally) ‚Äî too minor for its own tracked issue. Flagged #167 to #195 as a confounded
  data point (boundary held via orchestrator instruction, not the prose guard on its own).


## 2026-07-20 ‚Äî #168 ‚Äî xsd: Element Declaration component shape

- Shipped (commit `9441bfb`) the Element Declaration leaf shape in the `xsd`
  package: new `xsd.ElementDeclaration` (`xsd/elementdeclaration.go`), a
  `xsd.TypeTable` companion, and a shared `xsd.ScopeVariety` closed set
  (`xsd/closedsets.go`), with tests in `xsd/elementdeclaration_test.go` and
  additions to `xsd/closedsets_test.go`. Pure leaf shape ‚Äî the component the
  producer (#174) will fill and finalize (#173) will resolve; no cross-component
  resolution happens here.
- Grounded (oracle GROUNDING, issue #168): ¬ß3.3.1 Element_Declaration_details.
  Key seam calls: the `sc_e` Scope record is its OWN shape, deliberately NOT
  shared with attribute declaration's `sc_a` (they are distinct records in the
  spec, so no premature unification). e-props-correct clauses 1/3/6 are
  enforceable now on purely local state and are enforced; clauses 2/4/5/7 need
  resolved cross-component state and are deferred to finalize (#173).
- Warden PRE-FLIGHT: APPROVE WITH REVISIONS (planned-surface review, before code)
  ‚Äî load-bearing rulings: `TypeTable` modeled as its OWN type (not an inline
  field cluster); optional composition carried as value+bool rather than a
  pointer (D4, no nil-pointer illegal state); `ScopeVariety` given a SHARED name
  chosen for #169 (attribute decl) to reuse; and field/param ordering kept
  non-adjacent for same-typed neighbors to defeat silent argument transposition.
- Warden DIFF REVIEW: APPROVE WITH NITS (post-implementation) ‚Äî two non-blocking
  test-coverage gaps only: `Annotations()` copy-safety is not DIRECTLY asserted,
  and constructor input-slice aliasing is proven representatively but not for
  every slice parameter individually. Neither blocks; see Friction.
- Deliberately unmodeled at this leaf (each with a named later owner):
  `{scope}.{parent}` ‚Äî needs Complex Type Definition (#171) / Model Group
  Definition, which do not exist yet, so only global scope is fully
  constructible now; `{type definition}` and `{substitution group
  affiliations}` ‚Äî both stored as PRE-RESOLUTION QName references and resolved
  at finalize (#173), not here.
- Spec: xmlschema11-1 ¬ß3.3.1 (Element_Declaration_details), e-props-correct
  clauses 1/3/6 implemented (2/4/5/7 deferred to #173).
- Arbiter VERDICT: ACCEPT ‚Äî full gate green (build/test/vet/lint/conformance),
  no blocking STYLE findings. Ratchet run and confirmed unchanged via
  `GOXSD_RATCHET=1` with an empty `git status` afterward (no expectations file
  moved ‚Äî verified, not merely asserted).
- Ratchet: unchanged (arbiter ran the ratchet and confirmed no expectations lane
  moved).
- Friction: the two warden test-coverage nits (Annotations() copy-safety not
  directly asserted; slice-aliasing proven representatively, not per-parameter)
  remain open but non-blocking ‚Äî best picked up incidentally by whoever next
  touches `xsd/elementdeclaration.go`, not worth a standalone issue.
- Next: #169 (attribute declaration / group / use) is next in the M4 first-wave
  (#79) dependency order and MUST reuse the new shared `xsd.ScopeVariety` type
  per the pre-flight ruling. #170 (particle / model-group) also still unstarted
